PARAGRAPH_158292: Translation from Finnish Legally binding only in Finnish and Swedish Ministry of Justice, Finland

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:1]
PARAGRAPH_158293: Consumer Protection Act (38/1978; amendments up to 740/2022 included)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:1]
PARAGRAPH_158294: By decision of Parliament, the following is enacted:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:1]
PARAGRAPH_158296: General provisions

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:1]
PARAGRAPH_158298: This Act applies to the offering, selling and other marketing of consumer goods or services by traders to consumers. The Act also applies when a trader acts as an intermediary in the supply of goods or services to consumers.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:1]
PARAGRAPH_158299: This Act does not apply to statutory insurance or to employees' group life insurance or any corresponding benefit issued by a local government pensions institution.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:1] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158301: The provisions of this Act on sales shall also be applied to exchanges.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:1]
PARAGRAPH_158302: The provisions of chapters 3, 4 and 6 of this Act also apply to such contracts on consumer goods or services under which a consumer provides or undertakes to provide personal data to a trader, other than where the personal data is processed by the trader only for the purpose of supplying the consumer good or service or complying with any legal requirement to which the trader is subject. The provisions of chapter 2 of the Act apply to the offering, selling and other marketing of consumer goods or services also when the intention of the trader is for the consumer to provide or undertake to provide personal data and the trader does not process the personal data obtained only for the purposes referred to above in this subsection. Provisions on the application of the provisions of chapter 5a of the Act on such contracts on digital content or a digital service under which the consumer provides or undertakes to provide personal data to a trader are laid down in the said chapter. (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:2]
PARAGRAPH_158303: Section 2a (29/2005)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:2]
PARAGRAPH_158304: The provisions of chapters 3, 4 and 6a of this Act and the provisions of chapter 6 of this Act on off-premises sales apply, as appropriate, to undertakings given to lenders by private guarantors and private pledgors referred to in the Act on Guaranties and Third-Party Pledges (361/1999).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:2]
PARAGRAPH_158305: Section 3 (16/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:2]
PARAGRAPH_158306: For the purposes of this Act, consumer good or service means any goods, services or other commodities or benefits that are offered to natural persons or that are acquired by such persons in a material quantity for their private household.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:2]
PARAGRAPH_158307: Section 4 (16/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:2]
PARAGRAPH_158308: For the purposes of this Act, consumer means any natural person who acquires a consumer good or service primarily for a purpose other than trade carried out by the natural person.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:2]
PARAGRAPH_158309: Section 5 (16/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:2]
PARAGRAPH_158310: For the purposes of this Act, trader means any natural person or any private or public legal person that, to generate income or other financial benefit, professionally keeps for sale, sells or otherwise offers consumer goods or services to be acquired for consideration.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:2]
PARAGRAPH_158311: Section 6 (16/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:2]
PARAGRAPH_158312: Section 6 was repealed by Act 16/1994.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:2]
PARAGRAPH_158313: Chapter 2 (561/2008)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:2]
PARAGRAPH_158314: Marketing and practices in customer relationship

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:2]
PARAGRAPH_158315: Section 1 (561/2008)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:2]
PARAGRAPH_158316: Prohibition of marketing that is contrary to good practice and of unfair practices

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:2] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158317: Marketing shall not be contrary to good practice or use practices that are unfair to consumers. Neither shall unfair practices be used in a customer relationship.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:2]
PARAGRAPH_158318: Section 2 (561/2008)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:2]
PARAGRAPH_158319: Marketing that is contrary to good practice

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:3] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158320: Marketing shall be regarded as being contrary to good practice where it is clearly in conflict with generally accepted societal values and, in particular, where:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:3]
PARAGRAPH_158321: 1) it prejudices human dignity or is offensive to religious or political beliefs;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:3]
PARAGRAPH_158322: 2) it features discrimination on grounds of gender, age, ethnic or national origin, nationality, language, health, disability, sexual orientation or any other personal characteristic; or

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:3]
PARAGRAPH_158323: 3) it endorses activity that endangers health, public safety or the environment without any objectively justifiable reason associated with the marketed good or service for the presentation of such activity.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:3] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158324: Marketing that is targeted at or commonly reaches minors shall be regarded as being contrary to good practice particularly if it exploits the inexperience or credulity of a minor, if it is likely to have an adverse effect on the balanced development of a minor or if it aims to bypass the possibility of parents to fully exercise parental guidance of their child. When assessing whether marketing is contrary to good practice, the age and developmental stage and other circumstances of the minors commonly reached by the marketing shall be taken into consideration.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:3]
PARAGRAPH_158325: Section 3 (561/2008)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:3]
PARAGRAPH_158326: Unfairness of practices

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:3] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158327: A practice shall be regarded as unfair if it is:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:3]
PARAGRAPH_158328: 1) contrary to generally acceptable appropriate business practice; and

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:3]
PARAGRAPH_158329: 2) likely to clearly impair the consumer's ability to make an informed purchasing decision or other informed decision relating to a consumer good or service and to lead to the consumer making a decision the consumer would not have made without the practice.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:3] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158330: Practices that are contrary to sections 4-14 shall in particular be regarded as unfair.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:3] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158331: If a practice is targeted at a specific consumer group, the unfairness of the practice shall be assessed from the perspective of that consumer group. If a practice is likely to impair the decision- making of such consumers who are particularly susceptible to influence due to their age, disability or credulity, and the trader should have reasonably understood this, the unfairness of the practice shall be assessed from the perspective of that consumer group.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:4]
PARAGRAPH_158332: Section 4 (561/2008) Recognisability of marketing

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:4] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158333: Marketing shall clearly indicate its commercial purpose and on whose behalf the marketing is being carried out.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:4]
PARAGRAPH_158334: Section 5 (561/2008)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:4]
PARAGRAPH_158335: Risk of confusion

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:4] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158336: Comparative advertising or other marketing shall not create a risk of confusion between the trader's and a competitor's trademarks, trade names or other distinguishing marks, or goods or services if it is likely to lead to a consumer making a purchasing decision or other decision relating to a consumer good or service that the consumer would not have made without such marketing.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:4]
PARAGRAPH_158337: Section 6 (561/2008)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:4]
PARAGRAPH_158338: Prohibition of providing false or misleading information

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:4] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158339: In marketing or a customer relationship, false or misleading information shall not be provided if the information is likely to lead to a consumer making a purchasing decision or other decision relating to a consumer good or service that the consumer would not have made without the information provided.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:4]
PARAGRAPH_158340: False or misleading information may concern in particular:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:4]
PARAGRAPH_158341: 1) the existence, availability, type, quality, quantity or other main characteristics of a consumer good or service;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:4]
PARAGRAPH_158342: 2) the origin, method and date of manufacture, use and effects of use of, or the results of tests carried out on, a consumer good or service;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:4]
PARAGRAPH_158343: 3) the price of a consumer good or service or its determination criteria, or the existence of a specific price advantage or payment terms;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:4]
PARAGRAPH_158344: 4) the time of delivery and other terms of delivery of a consumer good or service;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:4]
PARAGRAPH_158345: 5) the nature of the selling practice, customer service after a contract has been concluded, and handling of customer complaints;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:4]
PARAGRAPH_158346: 6) the need for and availability of a service, repair or spare parts;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:5]
PARAGRAPH_158347: 7) the trader's or the trader's agent's identity, contact details, attributes and status in the market as well their awards and distinctions;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:5]
PARAGRAPH_158348: 8) the trader's rights and obligations, including undertaking to be bound by commitments contained in codes of conduct;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:5]
PARAGRAPH_158349: 9) the consumer's rights, obligations and risks; (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:5]
PARAGRAPH_158350: 10) a good being marketed as identical to a good marketed in other Member States, while that good has a significantly different composition or characteristics, unless justified by legitimate factors. (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:5]
PARAGRAPH_158351: Section 7 (561/2008)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:5]
PARAGRAPH_158352: Omission of relevant information

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:5] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158353: In marketing or a customer relationship, such information that, taking account of the factual context, is relevant and that the consumer needs to make a purchasing decision or other decision relating to a consumer good or service, and the omission of which is likely to lead to the consumer making a decision that the consumer would not have made with sufficient information, shall not be omitted.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:5] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158354: When assessing the sufficiency of information, the clarity, comprehensibility and timeliness of the information, the limitations of the communication medium used, and any other measures taken by the trader to make the relevant information available to consumers shall be taken into consideration.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:5] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158355: Any information that is necessary for consumer health and safety shall always be provided.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:5]
PARAGRAPH_158356: Section 8 (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:5]
PARAGRAPH_158357: Obligation to provide information when offering specified consumer good or service

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:5] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158358: Any marketing offering a specified consumer good or service at a specified price shall indicate:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:5]
PARAGRAPH_158359: 1) the main characteristics of the consumer good or service, to the extent appropriate taking account of the consumer good or service and the communication medium used;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:5]
PARAGRAPH_158360: 2) the name and geographical address of the trader and, where the trader is acting as an agent or representative of another trader, the same information concerning the trader's principal;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:6]
PARAGRAPH_158361: 3) the total price of the consumer good or service inclusive of taxes or, where the nature of the good or service is such that the exact price cannot reasonably be indicated, the price determination criteria;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:6]
PARAGRAPH_158362: 4) where necessary, any delivery charges not included in the total price or, where these charges cannot reasonably be calculated in advance, the fact that such charges may be payable;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:6]
PARAGRAPH_158363: 5) the policies for payment, delivery and performance of the contract if they depart from what consumers would normally have reason to expect; (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:6]
PARAGRAPH_158364: 6) any right to withdraw from or cancel the contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:6] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158365: Any marketing offering a specified consumer good or service on an online marketplace at a specified price shall also indicate whether the third party offering the good or service is a trader or not, on the basis of the declaration of that third party. (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:6]
PARAGRAPH_158366: Section 8a (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:6]
PARAGRAPH_158367: Information to be provided prior to concluding a contract

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:6] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158368: Besides other legal provisions elsewhere on the obligation to provide information, the trader shall, in transactions other than distance or off-premises selling of consumer goods or services, provide the consumer, before concluding a contract on a consumer good or service, with the following information in a clear and comprehensible manner if that information is not already otherwise apparent from the factual context:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:6]
PARAGRAPH_158369: 1) the main characteristics of the consumer good or service, to the extent appropriate taking account of the consumer good or service and the communication medium used;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:6]
PARAGRAPH_158370: 2) the trader's name, the geographical address at which the trader is established and the trader's telephone number;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:6]
PARAGRAPH_158371: 3) the total price of the consumer good or service inclusive of taxes or, where the nature of the good or service is such that the exact price cannot reasonably be indicated, the price determination criteria;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:6]
PARAGRAPH_158372: 4) where necessary, any delivery charges not included in the total price or, where these charges cannot reasonably be calculated in advance, the fact that such charges may be payable;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:7]
PARAGRAPH_158373: 5) where necessary, the terms concerning payment, delivery and other performance of the contract, and the customer complaints policy;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:7]
PARAGRAPH_158374: 6) a reminder of the existence of the trader's legal liability for any lack of conformity concerning goods, digital contents and services and, where necessary, a reminder of the availability and the conditions of after-sales services and guarantees; (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:7]
PARAGRAPH_158375: 7) where necessary, the duration of the contract or, where the contract is of indeterminate duration or is to be extended automatically, the conditions for terminating the contract;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:7]
PARAGRAPH_158376: 8) where necessary, the functionality, including applicable technical protection measures, of a good with digital elements and of digital content or a digital service, and any compatibility and interoperability of such a good or service that the trader is aware of or can reasonably be expected to be aware of. (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:7]
PARAGRAPH_158377: The provisions of this section do not apply to:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:7]
PARAGRAPH_158378: 1) a day-to-day contract for a consumer good or service which is performed immediately;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:7]
PARAGRAPH_158379: 2) a contract for a financial service or instrument;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:7]
PARAGRAPH_158380: 3) a contract for the sale or rental of immovable property or for any other right in immovable property;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:7]
PARAGRAPH_158381: 4) a contract under the scope of application of the Housing Transactions Act (843/1994);

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:7]
PARAGRAPH_158382: 5) a contract for the assignment of a right of occupancy referred to in the Right-of-Occupancy Housing Act (393/2021); (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:7]
PARAGRAPH_158383: 6) a residential lease agreement referred to in the Act on Residential Leases (481/1995);

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:7]
PARAGRAPH_158384: 7) a contract under the scope of application of chapter 10;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:7]
PARAGRAPH_158385: 8) a travel package referred to in the Act on Travel Service Combinations (901/2017); (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:7]
PARAGRAPH_158386: 9) a contract for passenger transport services;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:7]
PARAGRAPH_158387: 10) a contract for a service under the scope of application of the Lotteries Act (1047/2001);

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:8]
PARAGRAPH_158388: 11) a contract concluded by means of automated vending machines or automated commercial premises.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:8]
PARAGRAPH_158389: Section 8b (1699/2015)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:8]
PARAGRAPH_158390: Obligation to provide information on out-of-court dispute resolution entities

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:8] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158391: If the trader has a website, the trader shall provide on the website, in a manner that is easily accessible by consumers, clear and comprehensible, information on at least one such dispute resolution entity that has been notified to the European Commission in accordance with Article 20(2) of Directive 2013/11/EU of the European Parliament and of the Council on alternative dispute resolution for consumer disputes and amending Regulation (EC) No 2006/2004 and Directive 2009/22/EC and that is competent to deal with disputes between traders and consumers. The website address of the dispute resolution entity shall also be made accessible on the website. Corresponding information shall also be stated in any standard terms and conditions drawn up by the trader and submitted to the consumer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:8] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158392: If a lack of conformity concerning a consumer good or service has been brought to the trader's attention by a consumer and the parties have not reached an agreement on the matter, the consumer shall be provided with the information specified in subsection 1 in writing or on another durable medium.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:8]
PARAGRAPH_158393: Section 8c (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:8]
PARAGRAPH_158394: Special obligation to provide information at public auction of second-hand goods

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:8] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158395: At a public auction of second-hand goods, the trader shall make easily available to consumers clear and comprehensive information that the provisions of chapter 5 of this Act on the characteristics and lack of conformity of goods do not apply to the sale.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:8]
PARAGRAPH_158396: Section 8d (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:8]
PARAGRAPH_158397: Obligation to make available information on main parameters of results of search queries

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:8] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158398: When providing consumers with the possibility to search for consumer goods or services offered by different traders or private individuals on the basis of a query in the form of a keyword, phrase or other input, information shall be made available to the consumer on the main parameters determining the ranking of goods or services presented to the consumer as a result of the search query and the relative importance of those main parameters as opposed to other parameters. This

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:9] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158399: information shall be made available in a section of the online interface that is directly and easily accessible from the page where the query results are presented.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:9]
PARAGRAPH_158400: This section does not apply to providers of online search engines referred to in Article 2(6) of Regulation (EU) 2019/1150 of the European Parliament and of the Council on promoting fairness and transparency for business users of online intermediation services.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:9]
PARAGRAPH_158401: Section 8e (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:9]
PARAGRAPH_158402: Obligation to provide information about consumer reviews

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:9] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158403: Where a trader provides a consumer with access to consumer reviews of a consumer good or service, the consumer shall be provided with information about whether and how the trader has ensured that the published reviews originate from consumers who have actually used or purchased the good or service.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:9]
PARAGRAPH_158404: Section 9 (561/2008)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:9]
PARAGRAPH_158405: Prohibition of aggressive practices

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:9] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158406: Aggressive practices shall not be used in marketing or a customer relationship.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:9] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158407: Harassment, coercion or other application of pressure on the consumer that is likely to lead to the consumer making a purchasing decision or other decision relating to a consumer good or service that the consumer would not have made without the application of pressure shall be regarded as an aggressive practice.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:9] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158408: When assessing whether a practice is aggressive, account shall be taken, in particular, of:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:9]
PARAGRAPH_158409: 1) the timing, location, nature and persistence of the practice;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:9]
PARAGRAPH_158410: 2) the use of threatening or abusive language or behaviour;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:9]
PARAGRAPH_158411: 3) the exploitation of the consumer's misfortune or other such personal circumstance that impairs the consumer's judgement;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:9]
PARAGRAPH_158412: 4) any hampering of the exercise of the consumer's rights under the contract or law;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:9]
PARAGRAPH_158413: 5) any threat to take any action that cannot legally be taken.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:9]
PARAGRAPH_158414: Section 10 (561/2008)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:10]
PARAGRAPH_158415: Unsolicited supply of consumer goods or services

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:10] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158416: In marketing, consumer goods or services shall not be offered by supplying them to consumers without an explicit order and requiring any payment, return or safekeeping the good or service or any other measure from the consumer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:10]
PARAGRAPH_158417: Section 10a (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:10]
PARAGRAPH_158418: Requiring additional payments

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:10] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158419: Before the conclusion of a contract, the trader shall seek the consumer's express consent to any additional payments not included in the price indicated as payable for the consumer good or service. Any absence of the consumer's rejection of a default option used by the trader concerning the approval of an additional payment shall not be regarded as express consent.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:10] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158420: If the consumer has not provided express consent to an additional payment, the consumer shall not be obligated to make the payment.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:10]
PARAGRAPH_158421: Section 11 (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:10]
PARAGRAPH_158422: Announcements of price reductions on goods

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:10] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158423: When marketing a good at a discount or at a reduced price, the marketing shall also indicate the lowest price at which the good has been marketed during the period of 30 days prior to the price reduction. Where the price reduction is gradually increased in a marketing campaign the uninterrupted duration of which has not exceeded 60 days, the price indicated as the lowest price may be the lowest price at which the good has been marketed during the period of 30 days prior to the first price reduction.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:10]
PARAGRAPH_158424: The provisions of subsection 1 do not apply to perishable food.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:10]
PARAGRAPH_158425: Section 12 (561/2008) Bundled offers and offering of free gifts

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:10] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158426: Where in marketing consumer goods or services are offered at a single price or so that by purchasing a good or service one receives at a reduced price another good or service or another special benefit, the marketing shall clearly indicate:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:11]
PARAGRAPH_158427: 1) the content and value of the offer and, for goods or services offered at a single price, also their individual prices unless the individual price of a good or service when purchased separately is less than EUR 10;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:11]
PARAGRAPH_158428: 2) the terms of taking advantage of the offer, in particular the duration of the offer and any quantitative and other restrictions.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:11]
PARAGRAPH_158429: Section 13 (561/2008)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:11]

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:11] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158431: Where marketing includes prize draws, competitions for the public or games, the conditions for participation in them shall be clear, comprehensible and easily accessible.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:11]
PARAGRAPH_158432: Section 14 (1212/2020)

PARAGRAPH_158433: Charges payable for communication by telephone

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:11] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158434: The trader shall not, in communication by telephone in relation to a contract concluded by the trader concerning a consumer good or service, use a service for the use of which the consumer is required to pay charges exceeding the rate in accordance with the consumer's subscription contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:11] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158435: If the trader violates the provision of this section, the consumer shall have the right to receive from the trader compensation for any telephone costs exceeding the rate in accordance with the consumer's subscription contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:11]
PARAGRAPH_158436: Section 14 amended by Act 1212/2020 enters into force on 31 December 2023. Previous form of wording:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:11]
PARAGRAPH_158437: Section 14 (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:11]
PARAGRAPH_158438: Charges payable for communication by telephone

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:11] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158439: The trader shall not, in communication by telephone in relation to a contract concluded by the trader concerning a consumer good or service, use a service for the use of which the consumer is required to pay charges exceeding the rate in accordance with the consumer's subscription contract or charges exceeding the calculatory basic rate corresponding to the rate in accordance with the subscription contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:12] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158440: The calculatory basic rate is the rate based on telecommunications operators' minimum pricing and market shares plus 20 per cent. The Finnish Communications Regulatory Authority shall calculate and publish the calculatory basic rate annually. Further provisions on the calculation method and the publication of the basic rate are laid down by decree of the Ministry of Justice.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:12] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158441: If the trader violates the provision of this section, the consumer shall have the right to receive from the trader compensation for any telephone costs exceeding the maximum rate referred to in subsection 1.

PARAGRAPH_158449: Section 15a (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:12]
PARAGRAPH_158450: Consequences of violations of provisions on marketing and on practices in customer relationship

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:12]
PARAGRAPH_158451: If a trader has used an unfair practice referred to in the provisions of this chapter or a misleading or aggressive practice referred to in provisions laid down under section 15, paragraph 3 and the practice can be assumed to have influenced a purchasing decision made by a consumer, the consumer has the right request a price reduction that is reasonable relative to the trader's practice.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:12] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158452: A trader that intentionally or through negligence violates or fails to comply with the prohibition of unfair practice referred to in section 1 or the provisions of sections 4-8, 8d, 8e or 9 shall be obligated to compensate for the damage arising from this to the consumer. Likewise, a trader shall

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:13] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158453: be obligated to compensate for the damage caused by the trader having intentionally or through negligence used a misleading or aggressive practice referred to in provisions laid down under section 15, paragraph 3.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:13]
PARAGRAPH_158454: Section 16 (561/2008)

PARAGRAPH_158455: Prohibitory injunction

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:13] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158456: Where necessary for consumer protection, a prohibitory injunction may be imposed on a trader to refrain from continuing a practice in violation of provisions of this chapter or provisions laid down under them or from repeating such a practice or a corresponding practice. A prohibitory injunction shall be enforced by a notice of a conditional fine unless this is unnecessary on special grounds.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:13]
PARAGRAPH_158457: On special grounds, a prohibitory injunction may also be imposed on an employee or another person acting on behalf of a trader referred to in subsection 1.

PARAGRAPH_158458: Section 17 (561/2008)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:13]
PARAGRAPH_158459: Imposition of a prohibitory injunction

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:13]
PARAGRAPH_158460: A prohibitory injunction referred to in section 16 is imposed by the Market Court. The Market Court may also impose a prohibitory injunction on a provisional basis whereby the prohibitory injunction remains in force until a final decision has been taken on the matter.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:13]
PARAGRAPH_158461: The Consumer Ombudsman may impose a prohibitory injunction referred to in section 16 or impose a prohibitory injunction on a provisional basis as provided in section 10 of the Act on the Finnish Competition and Consumer Authority (661/2012). (684/2012)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:13]
PARAGRAPH_158462: Section 18 (1395/2009)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:13]
PARAGRAPH_158463: Prohibitory injunction imposed by Regional State Administrative Agency in certain matters

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:13]
PARAGRAPH_158464: A Regional State Administrative Agency may impose a prohibitory injunction referred to in section 16 in a matter pertaining to a practice in violation of provisions on the indication of the price of a dwelling or another consumer good or service if the unlawfulness is evident and there is an established practice in applying provisions in a matter of this kind. The decision by the Regional State Administrative Agency is ineligible for judicial review by appeal.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:14] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158465: A trader may refer a prohibitory injunction decision referred to in subsection 1 for consideration by the Market Court within fourteen days of having been notified of the decision. Otherwise the decision shall remain final.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:14]
PARAGRAPH_158466: The Regional State Administrative Agency may enforce a prohibitory injunction imposed by it by a notice of a conditional fine. The order to pay the conditional fine is made by the Market Court.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:14] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158467: Prior to imposing a prohibitory injunction referred to in subsection 1, the Regional State Administrative Agency shall give the trader the opportunity to be heard.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:14] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158468: When imposing a prohibitory injunction referred to in subsection 1, the Regional State Administrative Agency shall make its decision in writing and ensure it is served to the parties concerned.

PARAGRAPH_158469: Section 19 (561/2008)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:14]
PARAGRAPH_158471: When imposing a prohibitory injunction referred to in section 16, the Market Court may obligate the trader on which the prohibitory injunction was imposed, or which ordered or carried out the marketing, to rectify the marketing action within a time limit if this is to be regarded as necessary because of the evident harm caused to consumers by the marketing action. The order may be enforced by a notice of a conditional fine.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:15]
PARAGRAPH_158481: Regulation of contractual terms

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:15]
PARAGRAPH_158483: The trader may not, when offering consumer goods or services, use a contractual term that, taking account of the price of the consumer good or service as well as other relevant aspects, is to be regarded as unfair for consumers.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:15] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158484: If an association of traders draws up contractual terms relating to contracts for consumer goods or services or issues recommendations or instructions on terms to be used, the association shall ensure that its practice does not result in the use of terms that are unfair for consumers. (1259/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:15] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158486: Where necessary for consumer protection, a prohibitory injunction may be imposed on a trader to refrain from continuing the use of a contractual term that is in violation of section 1, subsection 1 or from repeating the use of such a contract term or a comparable contract term. A prohibitory injunction may correspondingly be imposed on an association of traders to refrain from continuing or repeating a practice in violation of section 1, subsection 2. A prohibitory injunction shall be enforced by a notice of a conditional fine unless this is unnecessary on special grounds. (1259/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:15]
PARAGRAPH_158487: On special grounds, a prohibitory injunction may also be imposed on an employee of, or another person acting on behalf of, a trader referred to in subsection 1.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:15]
PARAGRAPH_158489: A prohibitory injunction referred to in section 2 is imposed by the Market Court. The Market Court may also impose a prohibitory injunction on a provisional basis whereby the prohibitory injunction remains in force until a final decision has been taken on the matter. (1547/2001)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_158490: The Consumer Ombudsman may impose a prohibitory injunction referred to in section 2 or impose a prohibitory injunction on a provisional basis as provided in the Act on the Finnish Competition and Consumer Authority. (684/2012)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_158492: The use of contractual terms in respect of consumer protection is overseen by the Consumer Ombudsman.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_158493: Other provisions on the consideration of cases in the Market Court are laid down in the Market Court Proceedings Act. (133/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_158494: Chapter 4 Adjustment and interpretation of contract (1259/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_158495: Section 1 (596/2019)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_158496: If a term of a contract referred to in this Act is unfair for a consumer or if its application would result in unfairness, the term may be adjusted, unless otherwise provided in section 2, or it may be set aside. A commitment concerning the amount of consideration is also regarded as a term of a contract. When assessing unfairness, account is taken of the entire content of the contract, the position of the parties, the circumstances at the time the contract was concluded and, unless otherwise provided in section 2, any changes in the circumstances as well as any other factors.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_158497: If a term referred to in subsection 1 is such that, due to the adjustment of the term, it is not reasonable for the contract to remain in force unamended in other respects, the contract may, unless otherwise provided in section 2, be adjusted also in other respects or be ordered to lapse.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_158498: Section 2 (596/2019)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:16] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158499: If a contractual term referred to in section 1 was drawn up in advance without the consumer having been able to influence its content, the restrictions laid down in this section shall be complied with when applying the said section.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:16] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158500: If a term was unfair under the circumstances at the time the contract was concluded, any subsequent assessment of the unfairness of the term shall not, to the detriment of the consumer, take account of a change of circumstances.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:16] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158501: The unfair term shall be set aside and the contract shall in other respects be retained in force unamended if it can remain in force as such.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_158502: Section 3 (1259/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:17] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158503: If a term of a contract referred to in this Act was drawn up in advance without the consumer having been able to influence its contents, and there is doubt about the meaning of the term, the term shall be interpreted in favour of the consumer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_158504: Section 4 (1259/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_158505: In the event of a dispute over whether a term is a contractual term drawn up in advance referred to in sections 2 and 3, the burden of proof is on the trader.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_158506: Section 5 (416/1999)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:17] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158507: A choice-of-law clause under which the law of a non-European Economic Area state is applied to the contract shall not prevail over provisions in force in a Member State of the European Economic Area applied, in the absence of a choice-of-law clause, to unfair contract terms if these provisions provide consumers with more effective protection against unfair contractual terms than the law applied under the choice-of-law clause.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_158508: Chapter 5 (16/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_158509: Sale of goods (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_158510: General provisions on sale of goods (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_158511: Section 1 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_158512: Scope of application of chapter

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_158513: The provisions of this chapter apply to the sale of goods where the seller is a trader and the buyer is a consumer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_158514: The provisions of this chapter apply also to orders for goods to be manufactured or produced. If the buyer undertakes to supply a substantial part of the materials, sections 23-31 of chapter 8 apply, however, to the order instead of sections 23, 24, 24a, 24b, 25-28 and 28a of this chapter. In addition, the provisions of chapter 8, sections 14 and 32 apply to such orders. The provisions of section 29 of this chapter do not apply to such orders.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_158515: With the exception of sections 2, 2a and 3-11, the provisions of this chapter do not apply to public auctions of second-hand goods or to the sale of goods used exclusively as a carrier medium for digital content. Section 29, subsection 3 applies, in addition, to public auctions of second-hand goods.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:18]
PARAGRAPH_158516: The provisions of this chapter on guarantees also apply to any equivalent undertaking by the seller or the producer to the buyer at an extra charge. However, in such cases the seller is not liable under any undertaking by the producer for a lack of conformity for which the seller would not otherwise be liable under this chapter.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:18]
PARAGRAPH_158517: Section 2 (16/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:18]
PARAGRAPH_158518: Mandatory nature of provisions

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:18]
PARAGRAPH_158519: Any contractual term deviating from the provisions of this chapter to the detriment of the buyer is null and void unless otherwise provided below.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:18]
PARAGRAPH_158520: Section 2a (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:18]
PARAGRAPH_158521: Definitions relating to sale of goods

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:18]
PARAGRAPH_158522: For the purposes of this chapter:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:18]
PARAGRAPH_158523: 1) producer means a manufacturer of goods, an importer of goods into the European Union or any person purporting to be a producer by placing their name, trademark or other distinctive sign on the goods;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:18]
PARAGRAPH_158524: 2) sale of goods with digital elements means the sale of goods that under the contract incorporate or are inter-connected with digital content or a digital service supplied by the seller or a third party and the absence of that digital content or digital service would prevent the goods from performing their functions;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:18]
PARAGRAPH_158525: 3) functionality means the ability of the goods to perform their functions having regard to their purpose;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:18]
PARAGRAPH_158526: 4) compatibility means the ability of the goods to function with hardware or software with which goods of the same type are normally used, without the need to convert the goods, hardware or software;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:18]
PARAGRAPH_158527: 5) interoperability means the ability of the goods to function with hardware or software different from those with which the goods of the same type are normally used;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:18]
PARAGRAPH_158528: 6) public auction means a method of sale where goods or services are offered by the seller to buyers, who attend or are given the opportunity to attend the auction in person, through a transparent, competitive bidding procedure run by an auctioneer and where the successful bidder is bound to purchase the goods or services.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_158529: Delivery of goods and passing of risk

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_158530: Section 3 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_158531: Delivery of goods

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:19] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158532: Unless otherwise agreed, the goods shall be held collectible by the buyer at the place where the seller had the seller's place of business at the time of the conclusion of the sales contract. If the seller did not have a place of business relevant to the sale and if not otherwise agreed, the seller shall send or transport the goods to the buyer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_158533: The goods have been delivered when the buyer has acquired possession of the goods.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_158534: If the goods are to be installed or assembled by the seller at the buyer's premises, the goods are, however, when applying the provisions on the seller's delay or on the point in time determining lack of conformity, deemed to have been delivered only once the seller has fulfilled its said obligation. Correspondingly, in the sale of goods with digital elements, the goods are, when applying the said provisions, deemed to have been delivered only once the digital content or service has also been supplied to the buyer or, in the case of the continuous supply of the digital content or service over a period of time, the supply of the digital content or service to the buyer has begun.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_158535: If the buyer has commissioned a carrier proposed by the seller to transport the goods, the goods are, when applying the provisions on passing of risk, deemed to have been delivered only once the carrier has delivered the goods to the possession of the buyer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_158536: Section 4 (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_158537: Time of delivery

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:19] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158538: Unless agreed that the goods are to be delivered at a specified time or upon demand or without delay, the goods shall be delivered without undue delay and no later than 30 days after the conclusion of the contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_158539: Unless the buyer is granted credit or deferred payment, the seller is not obliged to transfer possession of the goods before the buyer pays the price of the goods.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_158540: Section 5 (16/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_158541: Costs incurred for goods prior to delivery

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:20]
PARAGRAPH_158542: Unless otherwise agreed, the seller is responsible for any transport costs and other costs incurred for the goods prior to their delivery. This, however, does not apply to any costs incurred because the delivery was delayed owing to a reason on the part of the buyer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:20]
PARAGRAPH_158543: Section 6 (16/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:20]
PARAGRAPH_158544: Passing of risk

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:20]
PARAGRAPH_158545: The seller bears the risk of any destruction, loss, deterioration or reduction of the goods prior to their delivery for a reason not attributable to the buyer. If the buyer fails to collect or receive in time the goods held available to the buyer, the buyer does, however, bear the risk of the deterioration of the goods due to their inherent characteristics after the seller has performed what the delivery requires of the seller.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:20]
PARAGRAPH_158546: If the goods are, due to a notification of a lack of conformity submitted by the buyer, returned to the seller for inspection or for remedy of the lack of conformity, the goods remain at the seller's risk until the goods are delivered back to the buyer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:20]
PARAGRAPH_158547: If a sale with option to return has been agreed upon and the goods have been delivered, the goods remain at the buyer's risk until the goods have been returned to the possession of the seller.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:20] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158548: If the goods are at the buyer's risk and the goods are destroyed, lost, deteriorated or reduced for a reason not attributable to the seller, the buyer shall, nevertheless, pay the price of the goods.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:20]
PARAGRAPH_158549: Consequences of delay in delivery of goods

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:20]
PARAGRAPH_158550: Section 7 (16/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:20]
PARAGRAPH_158551: Right to withhold payment

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:20]
PARAGRAPH_158552: The buyer has the right to withhold the payment of the price of the goods on the grounds of the seller's delay. The buyer may not, however, withhold any amount that manifestly exceeds the claims to which the buyer has the right on the basis of the delay.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:20]
PARAGRAPH_158553: Section 8 (16/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:20]
PARAGRAPH_158554: Right to require performance of contract

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:20]
PARAGRAPH_158555: In case of a delay in the delivery of the goods, the buyer has the right to require performance of the contract by the seller. The seller is not, however, obliged to perform the contract if there is an obstacle to performance that is insurmountable for the seller or if the performance of the contract would require sacrifices that are disproportionate to the significance of the performance of the contract to the buyer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:21]
PARAGRAPH_158556: Should the obstacle or disproportion end within a reasonable period of time, the buyer may, however, require performance of the contract by the seller.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:21]
PARAGRAPH_158557: The buyer loses the buyer's right to require performance of the contract if the buyer delays for an unreasonable period of time in presenting the requirement.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:21]
PARAGRAPH_158558: Section 9 (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:21]
PARAGRAPH_158559: Termination of sales contract

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:21]
PARAGRAPH_158560: The buyer may terminate the sales contract due to the seller's delay if the buyer has set a reasonable additional period of time for the seller and the seller has not delivered the goods within the additional period of time. Within the additional period of time set, the buyer may terminate the sales contract only if the seller has refused to supply the goods within that period of time.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:21]
PARAGRAPH_158561: The buyer may, however, terminate the sales contract due to the seller's delay without setting an additional period of time if:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:21]
PARAGRAPH_158562: 1) the seller has refused to supply the goods;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:21]
PARAGRAPH_158563: 2) delivery within the agreed supply period is essential, taking into account the circumstances relating the conclusion of the contract; or

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:21]
PARAGRAPH_158564: 3) the buyer has informed the seller prior to the conclusion of the contract that delivery by or at a specified time is essential.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:21] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158565: Upon the termination of the contract, the seller shall, without delay, reimburse all sums paid under the contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:21]
PARAGRAPH_158566: Section 10 (16/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:21]
PARAGRAPH_158568: The buyer has the right to damages for loss or damage suffered by the buyer as a result of the seller's delay, unless the seller demonstrates that the delay is due to an obstacle beyond the seller's control that the seller cannot reasonably be expected to have taken into account at the time of the conclusion of the sales contract and the consequences of which the seller could not reasonably have avoided or overcome.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:21]
PARAGRAPH_158569: If the delay is due to a person whose assistance the seller has enlisted for the performance of the contract or part of it, the seller is exempted from liability for damages only if also the said person

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:22]
PARAGRAPH_158570: would be exempt from liability under subsection 1. The same applies if the delay is due to the seller's supplier of goods or another previous link in the chain of transactions.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:22]
PARAGRAPH_158571: The seller is, however, obliged to compensate for indirect loss and damage to the buyer only if the delay, loss or damage is due to negligence on the part of the seller. Indirect loss or damage means:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:22]
PARAGRAPH_158572: 1) loss of income suffered by the buyer due to a breach of contract or measures resulting from a breach of contract;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:22]
PARAGRAPH_158573: 2) loss or damage due to an obligation based on another contract; and

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:22]
PARAGRAPH_158574: 3) essential loss of use of the goods not resulting in direct financial loss, as well as other comparable inconvenience that is material.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:22]
PARAGRAPH_158575: If the loss or damage referred to in subsection 3, paragraphs 1-3 is caused by the limitation of another type of loss or damage, it is not, however, considered indirect loss or damage in that respect.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:22]
PARAGRAPH_158576: A member of the buyer's family who suffers loss or damage due to a delay has the same right to compensation as the buyer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:22]
PARAGRAPH_158577: Section 11 (16/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:22]
PARAGRAPH_158578: Notice of termination of sales contract and claim for damages

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:22]
PARAGRAPH_158579: If the goods have been delivered late, the buyer may not terminate the sales contract or seek damages due to the delay unless the buyer within a reasonable period of time from the delivery of the goods notifies the seller or the intermediary in the sale that the buyer will terminate the sales contract or wishes to seek compensation. If the buyer terminates the sales contract, the buyer is not, however, obliged to provide a separate notice of a claim for damages.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:22]
PARAGRAPH_158580: Characteristics and lack of conformity of goods

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:22]
PARAGRAPH_158581: Section 12 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:22]
PARAGRAPH_158582: Characteristics of goods

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:22] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158583: The goods supplied by the seller to the buyer shall be in conformity with the contract. In order to conform with the contract, the goods shall, in particular:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:23]
PARAGRAPH_158584: 1) be of the description, type, quantity and quality and possess the functionality, compatibility, interoperability and other features as agreed under the contract;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:23]
PARAGRAPH_158585: 2) be fit for any particular purpose for which the buyer requires them and which the buyer made known to the seller at the latest at the time of the conclusion of the contract, and in respect on which the seller has given acceptance;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:23]
PARAGRAPH_158586: 3) be supplied with all accessories as well as installation and other instructions as stipulated by the contract;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:23]
PARAGRAPH_158587: 4) be updated as stipulated by the contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:23] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158588: In addition to the provisions of subsection 1, the goods shall comply with the following general requirements:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:23] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158589: 1) the goods shall be fit for the purposes for which goods of the same type would normally be used, taking into account applicable legislation, technical standards or, in the absence of these, sector-specific industry codes of conduct;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:23] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158590: 2) the goods shall be of the quality and correspond to any description of a sample or model that the seller made available to the buyer before the conclusion of the contract;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:23] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158591: 3) the goods shall be supplied along with any accessories, packagings as well as installation, user and other instructions that the buyer may reasonably expect to receive;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:23] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158592: 4) the goods shall be of the quantity and quality and possess the durability and other features normal for goods of the same type that the buyer may reasonably expect given the nature of the goods and taking into account any information provided by, or on behalf of, the seller, producer or any other person constituting a previous link in the chain of commercial transactions, when marketing the goods or otherwise before the time of the conclusion of the sales contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:23]
PARAGRAPH_158593: Section 12a (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:23]
PARAGRAPH_158594: Section 12a was repealed by Act 1242/2021.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:23]
PARAGRAPH_158595: Section 13 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:23]
PARAGRAPH_158596: General provision on lack of conformity

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:23]
PARAGRAPH_158597: If the goods deviate from the provisions of section 12, they lack conformity.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:24]
PARAGRAPH_158598: The goods are not, however, deemed as lacking conformity with the general requirements referred to in section 12, subsection 2:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:24]
PARAGRAPH_158599: 1) even if a particular characteristic of the goods was deviating from these requirements if, at the time of the conclusion of the contract, the buyer was specifically informed of the deviation and the buyer separately and expressly accepted that deviation when concluding the contract;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:24]
PARAGRAPH_158600: 2) if the lack of conformity or the defect is due to materials supplied by the buyer and used for the manufacture of the goods and the seller was not aware, nor should have been aware, of the lack of conformity of the materials.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:24]
PARAGRAPH_158601: The seller is also not liable for a lack of conformity relating to the provision of the information referred to in section 12, subsection 2, paragraph 4 if the seller demonstrates that:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:24]
PARAGRAPH_158602: 1) the seller was not, and could not reasonably have been, aware of the information in question;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:24]
PARAGRAPH_158603: 2) by the time of the conclusion of the contract, the information had been corrected in the same way as it had been provided or in a comparable way; or

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:24]
PARAGRAPH_158604: 3) the sales contract could not have been influenced by the information.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:24]
PARAGRAPH_158605: Section 13a (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:24]
PARAGRAPH_158606: Lack of conformity due to installation

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:24]
PARAGRAPH_158607: The goods also lack conformity if they due to incorrect installation deviate from the provisions of section 12 and the installation of the goods:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:24]
PARAGRAPH_158608: 1) is included in the sales contract and the goods were installed by the seller or someone else on the behalf of the seller; or

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:24]
PARAGRAPH_158609: 2) was under the buyer's responsibility and the incorrect installation carried out by the buyer was due to shortcomings in the installation instructions provided by the seller or, in case of the sale of goods with digital elements, in the installation instructions provided by the seller or the supplier of the digital content or service.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:24]
PARAGRAPH_158610: Section 13b (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:24]
PARAGRAPH_158611: Lack of conformity due to omission of updates in sale of goods with digital elements

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:25] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158612: In the sale of goods with digital elements, the seller shall ensure that the buyer is informed of and supplied with security and other updates that are necessary to keep the goods in conformity with the requirements laid down in section 12:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:25]
PARAGRAPH_158613: 1) for a period of time that is reasonable given the type and purpose of the goods and the digital elements and taking into account the circumstances and nature of the contract in the case of a single act of supply of digital content or a digital service; or

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:25]
PARAGRAPH_158614: 2) for the period of time during which the seller is liable for any lack of conformity of the goods and in any case for at least the period of time during which the digital content or service is to be supplied under the contract in the case of continuous supply of digital content or a digital service over a period of time.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:25]
PARAGRAPH_158615: If the seller has failed to carry out its obligations under subsection 1, the goods lack conformity.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:25]
PARAGRAPH_158616: If the buyer fails to install within reasonable time the updates supplied in accordance with subsection 1, the seller is not liable for any lack of conformity resulting from the lack of the relevant update, provided that:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:25]
PARAGRAPH_158617: 1) the seller informed the buyer about the availability of the update and the consequences of the failure to install it; and

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:25]
PARAGRAPH_158618: 2) the failure to install or the incorrect installation was not due to shortcomings in the installation instructions provided to the buyer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:25]
PARAGRAPH_158619: There is no lack of conformity within the meaning referred to in this section in goods with digital elements also if, at the time of the conclusion of the contract, the buyer was specifically informed that the buyer will not be informed of or supplied with updates in the manner required by subsection 1 and the buyer separately and expressly accepted that deviation when concluding the contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:25]
PARAGRAPH_158620: Section 14 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:25]
PARAGRAPH_158621: Lack of conformity due to third-party claim

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:25]
PARAGRAPH_158622: The goods also lack conformity if the goods are subject to a claim of a third party based on ownership, lien or other property right (lack of conformity due to a third-party claim) and the buyer is not obliged under the contract to accept the goods subject to the limitations arising from the third-party claim.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:26]
PARAGRAPH_158623: The buyer may rely on remedies provided for lack of conformity due to a third-party claim also when a third party asserts that they have a claim referred to in subsection 1 and there are reasonable grounds for the claim.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:26]
PARAGRAPH_158624: Section 15 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:26]
PARAGRAPH_158625: Time determining lack of conformity

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:26] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158626: Any lack of conformity of goods shall be assessed on the basis of the characteristics possessed by the goods at the time of delivery of the goods. The seller is liable for a lack of conformity in the goods that existed at that time, even if the lack of conformity only becomes apparent subsequently.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:26]
PARAGRAPH_158627: In addition to the provisions laid down in subsection 1, where the sales contract for goods with digital elements provides for a continuous supply of digital content or a digital service over a period of time, the seller is liable for a lack of conformity in the digital content or service which becomes apparent within the period during which the seller is liable for a lack of conformity in the goods or during which the digital content or service is to be supplied under the contract, whichever is the later. The seller is also liable for a lack of conformity due to omission of updates referred to in section 13b that becomes apparent within the period of time during which updates are to be supplied under section 13b, subsection 1.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:26]
PARAGRAPH_158628: Any lack of conformity which becomes apparent within one year from the time when the goods were delivered is presumed to have existed at the time when the goods were delivered, unless proved otherwise or unless the presumption is incompatible with the nature of the lack of conformity or with the nature of the goods. If a lack of conformity in digital content or a digital service to be supplied in a continuous manner over a period of time becomes apparent within the period of time during which the seller is liable, in the sale of goods with digital elements, under subsection 2 for a lack of conformity in the digital content or service, the lack of conformity is presumed to be a lack of conformity for which the seller is liable, unless the seller proves otherwise.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:26]
PARAGRAPH_158629: If the goods deteriorate after they have been delivered, the goods are deemed as lacking conformity if the deterioration is due to the seller's breach of contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:26]
PARAGRAPH_158630: Section 15a (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:26]
PARAGRAPH_158631: Guarantee and its relevance

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:26]
PARAGRAPH_158632: If the seller or someone on behalf of the seller has undertaken to be responsible, without any extra charge, for the usability or other features of the goods for a fixed period of time (guarantee),

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:27]
PARAGRAPH_158633: the goods lack conformity if the goods during that period of time deteriorate in accordance with the conditions specified in the guarantee statement and in advertising concerning the guarantee at or prior to the time of the conclusion of the contract. Liability for a lack of conformity does not, however, arise, if the seller can show that it is probable that the deterioration is due to an accident, incorrect handling of the goods or another matter on the part of the buyer.
