[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:27]
PARAGRAPH_158634: If the guarantee was provided by a party other than the seller constituting a previous link in the chain of transactions, the goods lack conformity also in that case, subject to the conditions referred to in subsection 1. The seller is not, however, liable on the basis of a guarantee provided by a previous link in the chain of transactions for a lack of conformity for which the seller would not otherwise be liable under this chapter if the seller demonstrates that the seller informed the buyer of the matter in a clear manner prior to the time of the conclusion of the sales contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:27]
PARAGRAPH_158635: If the conditions of the guarantee statement deviate from the conditions presented in advertising to the detriment of the buyer, the guarantee is binding in accordance with the conditions presented in the advertising, unless the advertising has been corrected in time in a manner that is the same or comparable to the manner in which the conditions were advertised.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:27]
PARAGRAPH_158636: A guarantee does not limit any liability for a lack of conformity laid down in this Act.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:27]
PARAGRAPH_158637: Section 15b (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:27]
PARAGRAPH_158638: Content and delivery of guarantee

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:27] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158639: A clear and comprehensible statement shall be drawn up concerning a guarantee and delivered no later than at the time of delivery of the goods to the buyer personally on paper or electronically in a way which allows its unchanged storage and reproduction by the buyer (guarantee statement).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:27] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158640: A guarantee statement shall include the following:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:27]
PARAGRAPH_158641: 1) the name and address of the guarantor;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:27]
PARAGRAPH_158642: 2) the designation of the goods to which the guarantee applies;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:27]
PARAGRAPH_158643: 3) the conditions of the guarantee;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:27]
PARAGRAPH_158644: 4) the procedure to be followed by the buyer to obtain the implementation of the guarantee;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:27]
PARAGRAPH_158645: 5) a clear statement that the buyer has legal rights and that those rights are not restricted by the guarantee.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:28]
PARAGRAPH_158646: The buyer has the right to rely on the guarantee even if the guarantee infringes the requirements laid down in this section.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:28]
PARAGRAPH_158647: Consequences of lack of conformity

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:28]
PARAGRAPH_158648: Section 16 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:28]
PARAGRAPH_158649: Buyer's rights

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:28]
PARAGRAPH_158650: If there is a lack of conformity in the goods for which the seller is liable, the buyer may require in accordance with the provisions of this chapter the correction of the lack of conformity, a new supply or a price reduction or terminate the sales contract and, in addition, claim damages. The seller may also withhold the payment of the price of the goods.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:28]
PARAGRAPH_158651: Section 16a (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:28]
PARAGRAPH_158652: Notification of lack of conformity

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:28]
PARAGRAPH_158653: The buyer may not rely on a lack of conformity unless the buyer notifies the seller of the lack of conformity within a reasonable period of time from the time the buyer detected or should have detected the lack of conformity. A notification of lack of conformity may, however, always be submitted within two months from the date on which the buyer detected the lack of conformity, and it may also be submitted to a trader acting as an intermediary in the sale on behalf of the seller or undertaking liability for the characteristics of the goods.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:28]
PARAGRAPH_158654: Notwithstanding the provisions of subsection 1, the buyer may rely on a lack of conformity in the goods if:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:28]
PARAGRAPH_158655: 1) the seller's conduct has been grossly negligent or incompatible with honour and good faith;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:28]
PARAGRAPH_158656: 2) the lack of conformity is based on the goods, in terms of their characteristics, lacking conformity with the requirements set for them under the Consumer Safety Act (920/2011) or other provisions or regulations issued to protect health or property; or

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:28]
PARAGRAPH_158657: 3) the lack of conformity is based on the goods otherwise posing a risk to health or property.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:28]
PARAGRAPH_158658: Section 17 (16/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:28]
PARAGRAPH_158659: Right to withhold payment

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:28] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158660: The buyer has the right to withhold the payment of the price of the goods on the grounds of a lack of conformity. The buyer shall not, however, withhold any amount that manifestly exceeds the claims to which the buyer has the right on the basis of the lack of conformity.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:29]
PARAGRAPH_158661: Section 18 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:29]
PARAGRAPH_158662: Remedy of lack of conformity

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:29] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158663: The buyer has the discretion to require that the seller either corrects the lack of conformity or supplies goods that are in conformity. The seller is not, however, obliged to remedy a lack of conformity in the manner required by the buyer, or at all, if there is an obstacle to this that is insurmountable for the seller or if this would incur disproportionate costs to the seller. Particular account shall be taken in this context of the significance of the lack of conformity and of the value of the goods in the absence of the lack of conformity as well as whether the remedy can be carried out in another manner without causing significant inconvenience to the buyer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:29]
PARAGRAPH_158664: The seller may not rely on the seller not having had the opportunity to remedy a lack of conformity if the buyer has had the lack of conformity corrected and, taking the circumstances into account, the buyer cannot be reasonably be expected to have waited for it to have been remedied by the seller.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:29]
PARAGRAPH_158665: Section 18a (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:29]
PARAGRAPH_158666: Procedure for remedying lack of conformity

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:29] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158667: The buyer shall make the goods to be corrected or replaced available to the seller. If the goods are to be replaced, the buyer may, however, refrain from returning the goods they have received until the new supply takes place. The buyer is not obliged to pay for the normal use of any goods that are replaced during the period prior to their replacement.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:29] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158668: The remedy of a lack of conformity shall be carried out within a reasonable period of time from the time the seller has been informed by the buyer about the lack of conformity and without any costs or significant inconvenience to the buyer, taking into account the nature of the goods and the purpose for which the buyer required the goods.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:29] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158669: The seller shall take back the replaced goods at the seller's expense. Where a correction or replacement requires the removal of goods that have been installed before the lack of conformity became apparent, the seller shall also take care of the removal of the goods lacking conformity and the installation of the conforming goods as well as bear the costs arising from these, provided that the goods have been installed in a manner consistent with their nature and purpose.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:29]
PARAGRAPH_158670: Section 19 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:29]
PARAGRAPH_158671: Price reduction and termination of sales contract

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:29]
PARAGRAPH_158672: The buyer may require a price reduction or the termination of the sales contract if:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:30]
PARAGRAPH_158673: 1) it is impossible to remedy the lack of conformity or this would result in disproportionate costs referred to in section 18, subsection 1;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:30]
PARAGRAPH_158674: 2) the seller has not remedied the lack of conformity or the remedy has not been carried out in the manner required under section 18a, subsection 3;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:30]
PARAGRAPH_158675: 3) the seller has declared or it is clear from the circumstances that the seller will not remedy the lack of conformity within a reasonable period of time or without significant inconvenience to the buyer;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:30]
PARAGRAPH_158676: 4) the lack of conformity in the goods appears despite the seller having attempted to bring the goods into conformity required in this chapter.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:30]
PARAGRAPH_158677: Notwithstanding the provisions of subsection 1, the buyer may require the price to be reduced or the sales contract to be terminated immediately if the lack of conformity is of such serious nature that remedying it is not possible.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:30]
PARAGRAPH_158678: The right to terminate the sales contract laid down in this section does not, however, exist if the lack of conformity is minor. The burden of proof with regard to whether the lack of conformity is minor is on the seller.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:30]
PARAGRAPH_158679: Section 19a (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:30]
PARAGRAPH_158680: Amount of price reduction

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:30] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158681: A price reduction shall be proportionate to the decrease in the value of the goods that were received by the buyer compared to the value the goods would have if they were in conformity with the requirements of this chapter.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:30]
PARAGRAPH_158682: Section 20 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:30]
PARAGRAPH_158683: Damages for lack of conformity in goods

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:30]
PARAGRAPH_158684: The buyer has the right to damages for any loss or damage suffered by the buyer due to a lack of conformity in goods. The seller is, however, liable in damages for indirect loss or damage referred to in section 10, subsections 3 and 4 above only if the lack of conformity and the loss or damage is due to negligence on the part of the seller or if the goods at the time of the conclusion of the sales contract deviated from a specific undertaking by the seller.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:30]
PARAGRAPH_158685: Notwithstanding the provisions of subsection 1, the buyer always has the right to damages for loss or damage due to a lack of conformity due to a third-party claim existing at the time of the conclusion of the contract that the buyer was not aware of, nor should have been aware of.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:31]
PARAGRAPH_158686: A member of the buyer's family who suffers loss or damage due to a lack of conformity has the same right to compensation as the buyer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:31]
PARAGRAPH_158687: Section 21 (16/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:31]
PARAGRAPH_158688: Product damage

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:31]
PARAGRAPH_158689: If a lack of conformity in goods causes damage to property other than the goods sold, the provisions of section 20 apply to the seller's liability in damages only if the damage is caused to property directly connected through a usage context with the goods sold.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:31]
PARAGRAPH_158690: If the seller pays damages under subsection 1, the possible right of the beneficiary to claim compensation for injury or damage under the Product Liability Act (694/90) is transferred respectively to the seller. The provisions of section 10 of the Product Liability Act also apply to the seller's right to damages.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:31]
PARAGRAPH_158691: The provisions of this chapter do not apply to compensation for personal injury due to characteristics of goods.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:31]
PARAGRAPH_158692: Section 22 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:31]
PARAGRAPH_158693: Liability in damages of parties other than seller

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:31]
PARAGRAPH_158694: If there is a lack of conformity in goods relating to the provision of information referred to in section 12, subsection 2, paragraph 4, the provisions laid down above on the seller's liability in damages apply to the information provider's liability in damages to the buyer for a lack of conformity.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:31]
PARAGRAPH_158695: If a party other than the seller has undertaken to remedy a lack of conformity in goods or to otherwise be liable for the characteristics of goods, the provisions laid down above on the seller's liability in damages apply correspondingly to the liability of the provider of the undertaking to compensate to the buyer for a non-fulfilment of the undertaking.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:31]
PARAGRAPH_158696: Section 22a (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:31]
PARAGRAPH_158697: Statute of limitations on claims for compensation

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:31]
PARAGRAPH_158698: Provisions on the limitation period for the buyer's claim for compensation are laid down in the Act on the Statute of Limitations on Debt (728/2003).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:31]
PARAGRAPH_158699: Buyer's obligations and consequences of buyer's breach of contract

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:31]
PARAGRAPH_158700: Section 23 (16/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:31]
PARAGRAPH_158701: Price of goods

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:32] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158702: If the price of the goods cannot be deemed as having been agreed, the buyer shall pay the price that is reasonable taking account of the quality and characteristics of the goods, the current price at the time of the conclusion of the sales contract as well as other circumstances. If the seller, when marketing the goods, has provided information on their price or on the price calculation method referring to the price level at the time of the conclusion of the sales contract that can be presumed to have influenced the sales contract, the price is determined in accordance with the information provided.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:32]
PARAGRAPH_158703: Section 24 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:32]
PARAGRAPH_158704: Time of payment

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:32] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158705: Unless otherwise agreed, the buyer shall pay the price of the goods upon request by the seller but not, however, before the goods are available to the buyer in accordance with the contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:32]
PARAGRAPH_158706: Before paying the price of the goods, the buyer has the right to inspect the goods in the usual manner or as appropriate considering the circumstances, unless the inspection is incompatible with the method of delivery and payment agreed.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:32]
PARAGRAPH_158707: If the payment is made through a bank or post office, when assessing the seller's rights under sections 26, 28 and 28a, the payment is deemed to have been made on the date when the bank or post office accepted the buyer's appropriate payment instruction.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:32]
PARAGRAPH_158708: Section 24a (1242/2021) Buyer's obligation to contribute

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:32] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158709: The buyer shall:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:32]
PARAGRAPH_158710: 1) contribute to the sales contract in the manner that can be reasonably expected of the buyer so that the seller is able to perform the contract; and

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:32]
PARAGRAPH_158711: 2) collect or receive the goods.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:32]
PARAGRAPH_158712: Section 24b (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:32]
PARAGRAPH_158713: Requirement to perform contract due to breach of obligation to contribute

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:32]
PARAGRAPH_158714: If the buyer fails to contribute to the sales contract in accordance with section 24a, paragraph 1, the seller has the right to remain in the contract and require that the buyer contributes to the sales contact in accordance with the said paragraph. The buyer is not, however, obliged to contribute to the sales contract if there is an obstacle to the contribution that is insurmountable for the buyer or if the contribution would require sacrifices that are disproportionate to the advantage gained by the seller from the buyer contributing to the sales contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:33]
PARAGRAPH_158715: Should the obstacle or disproportion end within a reasonable period of time, the seller may, however, require that the buyer contributes to the sales contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:33]
PARAGRAPH_158716: The seller loses the seller's right to require that the buyer contributes to the sales contract if the seller delays for an unreasonable period of time in presenting the requirement.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:33]
PARAGRAPH_158717: Section 25 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:33]
PARAGRAPH_158718: Requirement to perform contract in certain other cases

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:33]
PARAGRAPH_158719: If the buyer fails to pay the price of the goods at the right time, the seller has the right to remain in the contract and require that the price of the goods be paid.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:33]
PARAGRAPH_158720: If the buyer breaches the contract by cancelling the order for the goods prior to the delivery of the goods, the seller does not have the right to remain in the contract and require that the price of the goods be paid. Instead, the seller has the right to damages for any loss and damage suffered by the seller in accordance with section 28.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:33]
PARAGRAPH_158721: Section 26 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:33]
PARAGRAPH_158722: Seller's right to terminate sales contract due to late payment

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:33]
PARAGRAPH_158723: If the buyer is late in paying the price of the goods, the seller may terminate the sales contract if the breach of contract is material.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:33]
PARAGRAPH_158724: If the seller has set a specific additional period of time that is not unreasonably short for the payment of the price of the goods and the buyer fails to make the payment within the additional period of time, the seller may likewise terminate the sales contract. Within the additional period of time set, the seller may terminate the sales contract only if the buyer declares that the buyer will not make the payment within that period of time.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:33]
PARAGRAPH_158725: If the buyer has acquired possession of the goods, the seller may terminate the sales contract only if the seller has reserved the right to do so or if the buyer rejects the goods. Provisions on the seller's right to rely on a term concerning repossession of the goods when the buyer has been granted credit are laid down in chapter 7.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:33]
PARAGRAPH_158726: The seller may not terminate the sales contract due to the buyer's late payment after the late payment has been made.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:33]
PARAGRAPH_158727: Section 27 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:33]
PARAGRAPH_158728: Seller's right to terminate sales contract due to breach of obligation to contribute

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:34]
PARAGRAPH_158729: The seller may terminate the sales contract if the buyer fails to contribute to the sales contract in accordance with section 24a, paragraph 1 when the breach of contract is of essential significance to the seller and the buyer understood or should have understood this. The seller may terminate the sales contract under the same conditions if the buyer fails to collect or receive the goods at the right time and the contract or the circumstances indicate that it is of particular significance to the seller that the goods are taken away.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:34]
PARAGRAPH_158730: The seller may also terminate the sales contract if the buyer, within a specific additional period of time set by the seller that is not unreasonably short:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:34]
PARAGRAPH_158731: 1) fails to contribute to the sales contract in accordance with section 24a, paragraph 1; or

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:34]
PARAGRAPH_158732: 2) fails to collect or receive the goods when it is indicated by the contract or the circumstances that it is of particular significance to the seller that the goods are taken away.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:34]
PARAGRAPH_158733: Within the additional period of time, the seller may terminate the sales contract only if the buyer declares that the buyer will not fulfil their obligations within that period of time.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:34]
PARAGRAPH_158734: The seller may not terminate the sales contract due to the buyer having failed to collect or receive the goods unless the seller notifies the buyer of the termination before the buyer has fulfilled their obligations.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:34]
PARAGRAPH_158735: If the buyer has contributed to the sales contract in the manner referred to in section 24a, paragraph 1 but has done this too late, the seller may not terminate the sales contract due to the delay unless the seller notifies the buyer of the seller's request within a reasonable period of time from the seller becoming aware of the fulfilment of the obligation to contribute.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:34]
PARAGRAPH_158736: Section 28 (16/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:34]
PARAGRAPH_158737: Seller's right to damages

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:34]
PARAGRAPH_158738: If the seller terminates the sales contract due to the buyer's late payment before the buyer has acquired possession of the goods or if the buyer cancels the order for the goods in accordance with section 25, the seller has the right to compensation for any specific costs incurred by the seller from concluding and performing the contract and that are likely to be of no use, and for any specific costs arising from the termination of the sales contract or the cancellation.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:34]
PARAGRAPH_158739: As regards other loss or damage, the seller has the right to damages that are reasonable considering the price of the goods, the time of the termination of the contract or the cancellation, the measures taken to perform the contract as well as other matters.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:35]
PARAGRAPH_158740: A contract under which the seller reserves the right to a predetermined compensation due to a cancellation or termination is valid if the compensation in accordance with the contract is reasonable considering the compensation to which the seller generally would have the right under subsections 1 and 2.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:35]
PARAGRAPH_158741: The seller does not, however, have the right to a compensation referred to in this section if the buyer's late payment or cancellation of order is due to a provision of law, an interruption of general traffic or payment transactions or any other similar obstacle that the buyer cannot reasonably avoid or overcome.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:35]
PARAGRAPH_158742: Section 28a (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:35]
PARAGRAPH_158743: Interest for late payment

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:35]
PARAGRAPH_158744: If the buyer is late in paying the price of the goods, the seller has, where the sales contract is not cancelled or terminated, the right to receive interest for late payment in accordance with the Interest Act (633/1982).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:35]
PARAGRAPH_158745: Other provisions in sale of goods (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:35]
PARAGRAPH_158746: Section 28b (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:35]
PARAGRAPH_158747: Partial breach of contract

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:35]
PARAGRAPH_158748: If only a part of a supply is delayed or lacks conformity, the provisions on the breach of contract in question apply only to that part of the supply. The buyer may, however, terminate the sales contract in full if the buyer cannot be reasonably expected to accept only the part of the supply that conforms with the requirements of this chapter.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:35]
PARAGRAPH_158749: If it can be assumed that the seller considers that the seller has performed the contract in full even though not all of the goods have been delivered, the provisions on a lack of conformity apply.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:35]
PARAGRAPH_158750: Section 28c (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:35]
PARAGRAPH_158751: Termination of sales contract in cases of successive deliveries

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:35]
PARAGRAPH_158752: If the goods are to be delivered by instalments and an instalment of goods is delayed or lacks conformity, the buyer may terminate the sales contract concerning that instalment in accordance with the provisions that otherwise apply to the termination of sales contracts.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:35]
PARAGRAPH_158753: If the delay or lack of conformity gives reason to assume that a breach of contract entitling to termination will take place concerning a subsequent instalment of goods, the buyer may on such

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:36]
PARAGRAPH_158754: grounds within a reasonable period of time terminate the sales contract concerning such a subsequent instalment.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:36]
PARAGRAPH_158755: Section 28d (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:36]
PARAGRAPH_158756: Impacts of termination

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:36]
PARAGRAPH_158757: If the sales contract is terminated, the seller's obligation to hand over the possession of the goods and the buyer's obligation to pay the price of the goods and to contribute to the sales contract lapse.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:36] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158758: If the buyer exercises the buyer's right to terminate the sales contract, the buyer shall return the goods to the seller at the seller's expense, and the seller shall reimburse the buyer for the price of the goods once the seller has received the goods or evidence provided by the buyer of having sent back the goods.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:36]
PARAGRAPH_158759: Section 28e (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:36]
PARAGRAPH_158760: Benefit derived from goods

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:36] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158761: If the sales contract is terminated, the buyer shall hand over to the seller any proceeds obtained by the buyer from the goods and pay reasonable compensation if the buyer has derived any other benefit from the goods.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:36] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158762: If the seller must reimburse the price of the goods, the seller shall pay interest on the amount in accordance with section 3, subsection 2 of the Interest Act from the date on which the seller received the payment.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:36]
PARAGRAPH_158763: Section 29 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:36]
PARAGRAPH_158764: Application of Sale of Goods Act

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:36]
PARAGRAPH_158765: In addition, the provisions of section 8; section 9, subsections 2 and 3; section 46, subsection 1; sections 61 and 62; section 63, subsections 2 and 3; section 72; section 73, subsection 1 and sections 74, 79 and 82 of the Sale of Goods Act (355/1987) apply to sales contracts within the scope of application of this chapter. The provisions of section 66 of the said Act apply to the termination of sales contracts, and the provisions of sections 68 and 69 of the said Act apply to the buyer's right to compensation for a price difference.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:36]
PARAGRAPH_158766: The provisions of sections 75-78 of the Sale of Goods Act also apply to sales contracts within the scope of application of this chapter. The seller does not, however, have the right to damages under the said sections that are greater than provided in section 28 of this chapter. The provisions

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:37]
PARAGRAPH_158767: of section 76, subsection 2 of the Sale of Goods Act apply only where the seller has the duty to preserve the goods.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:37]
PARAGRAPH_158768: Notwithstanding the provisions of this section, the provisions of the Sale of Goods Act apply, however, to public auctions of second-hand goods unless otherwise provided by this Act.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:37]
PARAGRAPH_158769: Section 29a (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:37]
PARAGRAPH_158770: Section 29a was repealed by Act 1242/2021.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:37]
PARAGRAPH_158771: Section 30 (16/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:37]
PARAGRAPH_158772: Limitation of loss or damage and adjustment of damages

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:37] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158773: The party suffering loss or damage shall take reasonable measures to limit the party's loss or damage. Should the party fail to comply with this, the party itself shall suffer the corresponding share of the loss or damage.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:37]
PARAGRAPH_158774: Damages payable on the basis of a breach of contract may be adjusted if they are disproportionate taking account of the cause of the breach of contract, the counterparty's possible contribution to the loss or damage, the financial status of the contracting parties, the price of the goods, the possibilities of the party causing the loss or damage to anticipate and prevent the occurrence of the loss or damage, as well as any other circumstances.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:37] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158775: Damages that the buyer shall pay under section 28 may be adjusted particularly if the late payment or the cancellation of the order is due to payment difficulties encountered by the buyer owing to ill health, unemployment or any other reason that is primarily no fault of their own.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:37]
PARAGRAPH_158776: Section 31 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:37]
PARAGRAPH_158777: Liability of previous link in chain of transactions for lack of conformity

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:37]
PARAGRAPH_158778: The buyer has the right to direct their claim based on a lack of conformity in goods under the provisions of this chapter also against a trader that in a previous link in the chain of transactions has handed the goods over for resale.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:37]
PARAGRAPH_158779: The buyer does not, however, have the right specified in subsection 1:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:37]
PARAGRAPH_158780: 1) if the lack of conformity has arisen for a reason not attributable to the trader in question after the trader handed over the goods;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:38]
PARAGRAPH_158781: 2) to the extent that the claim is based on an undertaking provided by a party other than the trader in question that puts the buyer in a better position than the provisions of this chapter without the said undertaking;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:38]
PARAGRAPH_158782: 3) to the extent that the claim pertains to a price reduction or reimbursement of the price of the goods and its amount exceeds the amount that could have been claimed on the same grounds by the trader's own contracting party if not taking account of any restrictive conditions in an agreement between these.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:38]
PARAGRAPH_158783: The buyer loses their right to make claims under subsection 1 if the buyer fails to notify the lack of conformity to the trader or if the trader is not informed of a notification of lack of conformity submitted to a later link in the chain of transactions within the period of time laid down in section 16a, subsection 1 and if the information on the trader necessary for making the claim was available to the buyer. The buyer may, however, rely on a lack of conformity if the conduct of the trader against which the claim is made has been grossly negligent or incompatible with honour and good faith, or in the event of a lack of conformity referred to in section 16a, subsection 2, paragraph 2 or 3.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:38]
PARAGRAPH_158784: Section 32 (16/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:38]
PARAGRAPH_158785: Other trader's liability for lack of conformity

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:38]
PARAGRAPH_158786: If the seller has enlisted the assistance of another trader in the performance of the contract and there is a lack of conformity in that trader's performance, the provisions of chapter 8, section 35 on the right of the customer ordering a service to make claims against a trader whose assistance the contractor has enlisted applies correspondingly to the buyer's right to make claims against the trader whose assistance the seller enlisted.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:38]
PARAGRAPH_158787: Chapter 5a (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:38]
PARAGRAPH_158788: Contracts for digital content and digital services

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:38]
PARAGRAPH_158789: General provisions

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:38]
PARAGRAPH_158790: Section 1 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:38]
PARAGRAPH_158791: Scope of application of chapter

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:38]
PARAGRAPH_158792: This chapter lays down provisions on contracts under which a trader supplies or undertakes to supply to a consumer digital content or a digital service and:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:38]
PARAGRAPH_158793: 1) the consumer pays or undertakes to pay a price; or

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:39] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158794: 2) the consumer provides or undertakes to provide personal data to the trader, except where the personal data provided by the consumer is exclusively processed by the trader for the purpose of supplying the digital content or service in accordance with the provisions of this chapter or allowing the trader to comply with legal requirements to which the trader is subject.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:39]
PARAGRAPH_158795: Digital content means data which is produced and supplied in digital form. Digital service means a service that allows the consumer to create, process, store or access data in digital form or that allows the sharing of or any other interaction with data in digital form uploaded or created by the consumer or other users of that service.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:39]
PARAGRAPH_158796: With the exception of sections 5-9, this chapter also applies to contracts for the supply of such goods which serve exclusively as a carrier medium for digital content.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:39]
PARAGRAPH_158797: Section 2 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:39]
PARAGRAPH_158798: Limitations of scope of application

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:39]
PARAGRAPH_158799: The provisions of this chapter do not apply to contracts:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:39]
PARAGRAPH_158800: 1) that concern communications services referred to in the Act on Electronic Communications Services (917/2014), with the exception of number-independent interpersonal communications services referred to in the said Act;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:39]
PARAGRAPH_158801: 2) that concern a service within the scope of application of the Lotteries Act;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:39]
PARAGRAPH_158802: 3) that concern financial services or instruments;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:39]
PARAGRAPH_158803: 4) that concern software under a free or open-source licence where the consumer does not pay a price and the personal data provided by the consumer is exclusively processed by the trader for the purpose of improving the security, compatibility or interoperability of that specific software;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:39]
PARAGRAPH_158804: 5) on the basis of which digital content is made available to the general public other than by signal transmission as a part of a performance or event;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:39]
PARAGRAPH_158805: 6) that concern digital content provided by a public sector body in accordance with Directive (EU) 2019/1024 of the European Parliament and of the Council on open data and the re-use of public sector information.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:39]
PARAGRAPH_158806: Where a contract between the parties concerns both the supply of digital content or a digital service as well as other goods or services, the provisions of this chapter only apply to the elements

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:40]
PARAGRAPH_158807: of the contract concerning the digital content or service. In the case of the sale of goods with digital elements, however, the provisions of chapter 5 apply in full instead of the provisions of this chapter.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:40]
PARAGRAPH_158808: If the digital content or service is an element of a bundle of services referred to in section 108a of the Act on Electronic Communications Services, section 27 of this chapter does not apply.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:40]
PARAGRAPH_158809: Section 3 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:40]
PARAGRAPH_158810: Mandatory nature of provisions

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:40]
PARAGRAPH_158811: Any contractual term deviating from the provisions of this chapter to the detriment of the consumer is null and void unless otherwise provided below.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:40]
PARAGRAPH_158812: Section 4 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:40]
PARAGRAPH_158813: Definitions

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:40]
PARAGRAPH_158814: For the purposes of this chapter:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:40]
PARAGRAPH_158815: 1) integration means the linking and incorporation of digital content or a digital service with the components of the consumer's digital environment in order for the digital content or service to be used in accordance with the requirements laid down in this chapter;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:40]
PARAGRAPH_158816: 2) digital environment means hardware, software and any network connection used by the consumer to access or make use of digital content or a digital service;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:40]
PARAGRAPH_158817: 3) compatibility means the ability of the digital content or service to function with hardware or software with which digital content or services of the same type are normally used, without the need to convert the digital content or service;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:40]
PARAGRAPH_158818: 4) functionality means the ability of the digital content or service to perform its functions having regard to its purpose;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:40]
PARAGRAPH_158819: 5) interoperability means the ability of the digital content or service to function with hardware or software different from that with which digital content or services of the same type are normally used.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:40]
PARAGRAPH_158820: Supply of digital content or service and consequences of delay in supply

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:40]
PARAGRAPH_158821: Section 5 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:40]
PARAGRAPH_158822: Supply of digital content or service

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:41] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158823: Unless otherwise agreed, the digital content or service shall be supplied to the consumer without undue delay after the conclusion of the contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:41]
PARAGRAPH_158824: The trader has complied with the obligation to supply when:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:41]
PARAGRAPH_158825: 1) the digital content or any means suitable for accessing or downloading it is made available or accessible to the consumer or to a facility chosen by the consumer for that purpose;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:41]
PARAGRAPH_158826: 2) the digital service is made available to the consumer or to a facility chosen by the consumer for that purpose.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:41]
PARAGRAPH_158827: The burden of proof with regard to whether the digital content or service was supplied to the consumer in the manner required by this section is on the trader.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:41]
PARAGRAPH_158828: Section 6 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:41]
PARAGRAPH_158829: Right to withhold payment

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:41] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158830: The consumer has the right to withhold the payment of the price on the grounds of the trader's delay. The consumer shall not, however, withhold any amount of the price that manifestly exceeds the claims to which the consumer has the right on the basis of the delay.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:41]
PARAGRAPH_158831: Section 7 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:41]
PARAGRAPH_158832: Right to require performance of contract

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:41]
PARAGRAPH_158833: In the event of a delay in the supply of the digital content or service, the consumer has the right to require performance of the contract by the trader. The trader is not, however, obliged to perform the contract if there is an obstacle to the performance that is insurmountable for the trader or if the performance of the contract would require sacrifices that are disproportionate to the significance of the performance of the contract to the consumer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:41]
PARAGRAPH_158834: Should the obstacle or disproportion end within a reasonable period of time, the consumer may, however, require performance of the contract by the trader.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:41]
PARAGRAPH_158835: The consumer loses their right to require performance of the contract if the consumer delays for an unreasonable period of time in presenting the requirement.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:41]
PARAGRAPH_158836: Section 8 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:41]
PARAGRAPH_158837: Termination of contract

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:41]
PARAGRAPH_158838: The consumer may terminate the contract due to the trader's delay if the consumer has requested the supply of the digital content or service by the trader and the trader has failed to supply it

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:42]
PARAGRAPH_158839: without undue delay or within an additional period of time expressly agreed to by the parties. The consumer may terminate the contract within the agreed additional time only if the trader has declared, or it is clear from the circumstances, that the trader will not supply the digital content or service within that period of time.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:42]
PARAGRAPH_158840: The consumer may, however, terminate the contract due to the trader's delay without agreeing upon an additional period of time if:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:42]
PARAGRAPH_158841: 1) the trader has declared, or it is clear from the circumstances, that the trader will not supply the digital content or service;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:42]
PARAGRAPH_158842: 2) the parties have stated in consensus that supply at or by a specific time is essential for the consumer;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:42]
PARAGRAPH_158843: 3) taking account of the circumstances relating to the conclusion of the contract, it is clear that supply at or by a specific time is essential.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:42]
PARAGRAPH_158844: The provisions of sections 24-26 apply to the termination of contracts.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:42]
PARAGRAPH_158845: Section 9 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:42]
PARAGRAPH_158846: Damages for delay

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:42]
PARAGRAPH_158847: The consumer has the right to damages for loss or damage suffered by the consumer as a result of the trader's delay, unless the trader demonstrates that the delay is due to an obstacle beyond the trader's control that the trader cannot reasonably be expected to have taken into account at the time of the conclusion of the contract and the consequences of which the trader could also not reasonably have avoided or overcome.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:42]
PARAGRAPH_158848: If the delay is due to a person whose assistance the trader has enlisted for the performance of the contract or part of it, the trader is exempted from liability in damages only if also the said person would be exempt from liability under subsection 1. The same applies if the delay is due to a previous link in the chain of transactions.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:42] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158849: The trader shall, however, be obliged to compensate for indirect loss and damage to the consumer only if the delay, loss or damage is due to negligence on the part of the trader. Indirect loss or damage means:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:42]
PARAGRAPH_158850: 1) loss of income suffered by the consumer due to a breach of contract or measures resulting from a breach of contract;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:43]
PARAGRAPH_158851: 2) loss or damage due to an obligation based on another contract; and

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:43]
PARAGRAPH_158852: 3) essential loss of use of the digital content or service not resulting in direct financial loss, as well as other comparable inconvenience that is material.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:43]
PARAGRAPH_158853: If the loss or damage referred to in subsection 3 is caused by the limitation of other loss or damage, it is not, however, considered indirect loss or damage in that respect.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:43]
PARAGRAPH_158854: A member of the consumer's family who suffers loss or damage due to a delay has the same right to compensation as the buyer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:43]
PARAGRAPH_158855: Characteristics and lack of conformity of digital content or service

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:43]
PARAGRAPH_158856: Section 10 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:43]
PARAGRAPH_158857: Characteristics of digital content or service

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:43] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158858: The digital content or service supplied by the trader to the consumer shall be in conformity with the contract. In order to conform with the contract, it shall, in particular:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:43]
PARAGRAPH_158859: 1) be of the description, quantity and quality and possess the functionality, compatibility, interoperability and other features as agreed under the contract;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:43]
PARAGRAPH_158860: 2) be fit for any particular purpose for which the consumer requires it and which the consumer made known to the trader at the latest at the time of the conclusion of the contract, and in respect on which the trader has given acceptance;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:43]
PARAGRAPH_158861: 3) be supplied with all accessories as well as installation and other instructions as stipulated by the contract;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:43]
PARAGRAPH_158862: 4) be supplied with customer support as stipulated by the contract;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:43]
PARAGRAPH_158863: 5) be updated as stipulated by the contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:43] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158864: In addition to the provisions of subsection 1, the digital content or service shall comply with the following general requirements:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:43] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158865: 1) the digital content or service shall be fit for the purposes for which digital content or a digital service of the same type would normally be used, taking into account applicable legislation, technical standards or, in the absence of these, sector-specific industry codes of conduct;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:44] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158866: 2) the digital content or service shall be of the quantity and quality and possess the performance and other features in relation to functionality, compatibility, accessibility, continuity and security normal for digital content or a digital service of the same type which the consumer may reasonably expect, given the nature of the digital content or service and taking into account any information provided by, or on behalf of, the trader or any other person in a previous link in the chain of commercial transactions, when marketing the digital content or service or otherwise before the time of the conclusion of the contract;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:44] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158867: 3) the digital content or service shall be supplied along with the necessary accessories and instructions which the consumer may reasonably expect to receive;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:44] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158868: 4) the digital content or service shall comply with any trial version or preview made available to the consumer by the trader before the conclusion of the contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:44] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158869: Unless otherwise agreed, the digital content or service shall also be supplied in the most recent version available at the time of the conclusion of the contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:44]
PARAGRAPH_158870: Section 11 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:44]
PARAGRAPH_158871: General provision on lack of conformity

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:44]
PARAGRAPH_158872: If the digital content or service deviates from the provisions of section 10, it lacks conformity.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:44]
PARAGRAPH_158873: Digital content or a digital service is not, however, deemed as lacking conformity with the general requirements referred to in section 10, subsection 2 even if a particular characteristic of the digital content or service deviates from those requirements if the consumer at the time of the conclusion of the contract was specifically informed of the deviation and the consumer separately and expressly accepted that deviation when concluding the contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:44]
PARAGRAPH_158874: The trader is also not liable for a lack of conformity relating to the provision of the information referred to in section 10, subsection 2, paragraph 2 if the trader demonstrates that:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:44]
PARAGRAPH_158875: 1) the trader was not, and could not reasonably have been, aware of the information in question;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:44]
PARAGRAPH_158876: 2) by the time of the conclusion of the contract, the information had been corrected in the same way as it had been provided or in a comparable way; or

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:44]
PARAGRAPH_158877: 3) the consumer's decision to conclude the contract could not have been influenced by the information.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:45]
PARAGRAPH_158878: Section 12 (1242/2021) Lack of conformity due to omission of updates concerning digital content or services

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:45] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158879: The trader shall ensure that the consumer is informed of and supplied with security and other updates that are necessary to keep the digital content or service in conformity with the requirements laid down in section 10:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:45]
PARAGRAPH_158880: 1) for a period of time that is reasonable, given the type and purpose of the digital content or service and taking into account the circumstances and nature of the contract, in the case of a single act of supply or a series of individual acts of supply of digital content or a digital service;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:45]
PARAGRAPH_158881: 2) for the period of time during which the digital content or service is to be supplied to the consumer under the contract in the case of a continuous supply of digital content or service over a period of time.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:45]
PARAGRAPH_158882: If the trader has failed to carry out its obligations under subsection 1, the digital content or service lacks conformity.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:45]
PARAGRAPH_158883: If the consumer fails to install within a reasonable period of time the updates supplied in accordance with subsection 1, the trader is not liable for any lack of conformity resulting solely from the lack of the relevant update, provided that:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:45]
PARAGRAPH_158884: 1) the trader informed the consumer about the availability of the update and the consequences of the failure to install it; and

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:45]
PARAGRAPH_158885: 2) the failure to install or the incorrect installation was not due to shortcomings in the installation instructions provided to the consumer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:45]
PARAGRAPH_158886: There is, however, no lack of conformity within the meaning referred to in this section in digital content or a digital service if, at the time of the conclusion of the contract, the consumer was specifically informed that the consumer will not be informed of or supplied with updates in the manner required by subsection 1 and the consumer separately and expressly accepted that deviation when concluding the contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:45]
PARAGRAPH_158887: Section 13 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:45]
PARAGRAPH_158888: Lack of conformity due to integration

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:45]
PARAGRAPH_158889: The digital content or service also lacks conformity if, due to incorrect integration, it deviates from the provisions of section 10, and:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:46]
PARAGRAPH_158890: 1) the trader was responsible for the integration of the digital content or service; or

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:46]
PARAGRAPH_158891: 2) the consumer was responsible for the integration of the digital content or service and the incorrect integration was due to shortcomings in the integration instructions provided by the trader.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:46]
PARAGRAPH_158892: Section 14 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:46]
PARAGRAPH_158893: Lack of conformity due to third-party claim

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:46]
PARAGRAPH_158894: Digital content or a digital service also lacks conformity if a good used as a carrier medium for the digital content is subject to a claim of a third party based on ownership, lien or other property right (lack of conformity due to a third-party claim) and the consumer is not obliged under the contract to accept the good subject to the limitations arising from the third-party claim.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:46]
PARAGRAPH_158895: The consumer may rely on the remedies provided for lack of conformity due to a third-party claim also when a third party asserts that the third party has a claim referred to in subsection 1 and there are probable grounds for the claim.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:46]
PARAGRAPH_158896: Section 15 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:46]
PARAGRAPH_158897: Time determining lack of conformity

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:46]
PARAGRAPH_158898: In the case of a single act of supply or a series of individual acts of supply of digital content or a digital service, the trader is liable for a lack of conformity in the digital content or service that existed at the time of supply of the digital content or service even if the lack of conformity only becomes apparent subsequently.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:46]
PARAGRAPH_158899: In the case of a continuous supply of digital content or service over a period time, the trader is liable for a lack of conformity which becomes apparent within the period of time during which the digital content or service is to be supplied under the contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:46]
PARAGRAPH_158900: The trader is also liable for a lack of conformity, due to omission of updates referred to in section 12, which becomes apparent within the period of time during which updates are to be supplied under section 12, subsection 1.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:46]
PARAGRAPH_158901: Section 16 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:46]
PARAGRAPH_158902: Presumption of lack of conformity

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:46]
PARAGRAPH_158903: In the case of a single act of supply or a series of individual acts of supply of digital content or a digital service, the lack of conformity is presumed to have existed at the time of supply if it becomes apparent within one year from that time, unless the trader proves otherwise. In the case of a continuous supply of digital content or a digital service over a period time where the lack of

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:47]
PARAGRAPH_158904: conformity becomes apparent during that period of time, the trader is presumed to be liable for the lack of conformity, unless the trader proves otherwise.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:47]
PARAGRAPH_158905: The provisions of subsection 1 do not apply if the trader proves that the digital environment of the consumer is not compatible with the technical requirements of the digital content or service and the consumer was informed of such requirements in a clear and comprehensible manner before the conclusion of the contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:47] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158906: The consumer shall cooperate with the trader, to the extent that is reasonable and necessary, to ascertain whether the cause of the lack of conformity of the digital content or service lay in the consumer's digital environment. Where the trader informed the consumer of the requirement to cooperate in a clear and comprehensible manner before the conclusion of the contract but the consumer fails to cooperate, the provisions of subsection 1 do not apply in that case, either.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:47]
PARAGRAPH_158907: Consequences of lack of conformity

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:47]
PARAGRAPH_158908: Section 17 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:47]
PARAGRAPH_158909: Consumer's rights in the event of lack of conformity

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:47]
PARAGRAPH_158910: In the event of a lack of conformity for which the trader is liable in the digital content or service, the consumer may, in accordance with the provisions of this chapter, require the remedying of the lack of conformity or a price reduction or terminate the contract and, in addition, seek damages. The consumer may also withhold the payment of the price.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:47]
PARAGRAPH_158911: The consumer's right to rely on the remedies laid down in this chapter against the trader does not affect the trader's right to pursue remedies against a party liable for the lack of conformity in a previous link in the chain of commercial transactions.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:47]
PARAGRAPH_158912: Section 18 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:47]
PARAGRAPH_158913: Right to withhold payment

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:47] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158914: The consumer has the right to withhold the payment of the price on the grounds of a lack of conformity. The consumer shall not, however, withhold any amount that manifestly exceeds the claims to which the consumer has the right on the basis of the lack of conformity.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:47]
PARAGRAPH_158915: Section 19 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:47]
PARAGRAPH_158916: Remedy of lack of conformity

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:47] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158917: The consumer has the right to require the remedy of a lack of conformity. The remedy shall be carried out within a reasonable period of time and without causing the consumer any costs or

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:48]
PARAGRAPH_158918: significant inconvenience, taking account of the nature of the digital content or service and the purpose for which the consumer required the digital content or service.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:48] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158919: The trader is not, however, obliged to remedy a lack of conformity if there is an obstacle to this that is insurmountable for the trader or if this would incur disproportionate costs to the trader. Particular account shall be taken in this of the significance of the lack of conformity and of the value of the digital content or service in the absence of the lack of conformity.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:48]
PARAGRAPH_158920: Section 20 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:48]
PARAGRAPH_158921: Price reduction and termination of contract

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:48]
PARAGRAPH_158922: The consumer may require a price reduction provided that the digital content or service is supplied in exchange for a payment of a price, or terminate the contract, if:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:48]
PARAGRAPH_158923: 1) the remedy of the lack of conformity is not possible for reasons referred to in section 19, subsection 2;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:48]
PARAGRAPH_158924: 2) the trader has not remedied the lack of conformity in the manner required by section 19, subsection 1;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:48]
PARAGRAPH_158925: 3) the trader has declared, or it is clear from the circumstances, that the trader will not remedy the lack of conformity within a reasonable time or without significant inconvenience to the consumer;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:48]
PARAGRAPH_158926: 4) the lack of conformity of the digital content or service appears despite the trader's attempt to bring the digital content or service into conformity as required in this chapter.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:48]
PARAGRAPH_158927: Notwithstanding the provisions of subsection 1, the consumer may require the price to be reduced provided that the digital content or service is supplied in exchange for a payment of a price, or the contract to be terminated immediately, if the lack of conformity is of such serious nature that remedying it is not possible.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:48]
PARAGRAPH_158928: If the digital content or service is supplied in exchange for the payment of a price, the right to terminate the contract does not, however, exist if the lack of conformity is minor. The burden of proof with regard to whether the lack of conformity is minor is on the trader.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:48]
PARAGRAPH_158929: Section 21 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:48]
PARAGRAPH_158930: Determination of price reduction

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:49] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158931: The price reduction shall be proportionate to the decrease in the value of the digital content or service which was supplied to the consumer compared to the value that the digital content or service would have if it were in conformity with the requirements of this chapter.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:49]
PARAGRAPH_158932: In the case of a continuous supply of digital content or a digital service over a period time, the right to a price reduction applies to the period of time during which the digital content or service has not been in conformity.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:49]
PARAGRAPH_158933: Section 22 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:49]
PARAGRAPH_158934: Damages for lack of conformity

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:49]
PARAGRAPH_158935: The consumer has the right to damages for any loss or damage suffered by the consumer due to a lack of conformity in digital content or a digital service. The liability in damages covers personal injury, damage to property and financial loss suffered by the consumer due to the lack of conformity. The trader is, however, liable in damages for indirect loss or damage referred to in section 9, subsections 3 and 4 above only if the lack of conformity or the loss or damage is due to negligence on the part of the trader or if the digital content or service at the time of the conclusion of the contract or, in the case of the supply of digital content or service over a period of time, during that period of time deviated from a specific undertaking by the trader.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:49]
PARAGRAPH_158936: Notwithstanding the provisions of subsection 1, the consumer always has the right to damages for loss or damage due to a lack of conformity due to a third-party claim existing at the time of the conclusion of the contract that the consumer was not aware of, nor should have been aware of.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:49]
PARAGRAPH_158937: A member of the consumer's family who suffers loss or damage due to a lack of conformity has the same right to compensation as the consumer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:49]
PARAGRAPH_158938: Section 23 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:49]
PARAGRAPH_158939: Damage to other property

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:49]
PARAGRAPH_158940: If a lack of conformity in digital content or a digital service causes damage to other property, the provisions of section 22 apply to the trader's liability in damages only if the damage is caused to property directly connected through a usage context with the digital content or service.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:49]
PARAGRAPH_158941: If the trader pays damages under subsection 1, any right of the beneficiary to claim compensation for injury or damage under the Product Liability Act is transferred respectively to the trader. The provisions of section 10 of the Product Liability Act also apply to the trader's right to damages.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:49]
PARAGRAPH_158942: Impacts of termination of contract

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:50]
PARAGRAPH_158943: Section 24 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:50]
PARAGRAPH_158944: Impacts of termination of contract on payments

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:50]
PARAGRAPH_158945: In the event of the termination of the contract, the trader is obliged to reimburse the consumer for all sums paid under the contract. However, in cases where the contract provides for the supply of the digital content or service in exchange for a payment of a price and over a period of time, and the digital content or service had been in conformity with the requirements of this chapter for a period of time prior to the termination of the contract, the trader is obliged to reimburse the consumer only for the part of the price paid corresponding to the period of time during which the digital content or service was not in conformity with the requirements of this chapter, and any part of the price paid by the consumer in advance for any period of the contract that would have remained had the contract not been terminated.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:50]
