PARAGRAPH_158946: The consumer is not liable to pay for any use made of the digital content or service in the period, prior to the termination of the contract, during which the digital content or service was not in conformity with the requirements of this chapter.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:50]
PARAGRAPH_158947: Section 25 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:50]
PARAGRAPH_158948: Impacts of termination of contract on use of digital content or service

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:50] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158949: In the event of the termination of the contract, the consumer shall refrain from using the digital content or service and from making it available to third parties. Where the digital content was supplied on a carrier medium, the consumer shall, at the request and at the expense of the trader, return the medium to the trader without undue delay. The trader shall make that request within 14 days from the date on which the trader is informed of the consumer's decision to terminate the contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:50]
PARAGRAPH_158950: When the contract is terminated, the trader has the right to make the digital content or service inaccessible by the consumer, disable the user account of the consumer or in another manner prevent the use of the digital content or service by the consumer, unless otherwise provided in subsection 4.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:50] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158951: The trader shall refrain from using the content which was provided or created by the consumer through the use of the digital content or service supplied by the trader unless:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:50]
PARAGRAPH_158952: 1) the content has no utility outside the context of the digital content or service supplied by the trader;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:51]
PARAGRAPH_158953: 2) the content only relates to the consumer's activity when using the digital content or service supplied by the trader;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:51]
PARAGRAPH_158954: 3) the content has been aggregated with other data by the trader and cannot be disaggregated or only with disproportionate efforts; or

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:51]
PARAGRAPH_158955: 4) the content has been generated jointly by the consumer and other consumers, and other consumers are able to continue to make use of the content.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:51] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158956: In cases other than those referred to in subsection 3, paragraphs 1-3, the trader shall, at the request of the consumer, make available to the consumer any content which was provided or created by the consumer when using the digital content or service supplied by the trader. This shall be provided free of charge within a reasonable time and in a commonly used and machine- readable format.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:51]
PARAGRAPH_158957: The provisions of subsections 3 and 4 do not apply to personal data. Provisions on the use of personal data are laid down in Regulation (EU) 2016/679 of the European Parliament and of the Council on the protection of natural persons with regard to the processing of personal data and on the free movement of such data, and repealing Directive 95/46/EC ( General Data Protection Regulation).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:51]
PARAGRAPH_158958: Other provisions

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:51]
PARAGRAPH_158959: Section 26 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:51]
PARAGRAPH_158960: Reimbursement of payments

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:51] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158961: Any reimbursement of payments laid down in this chapter shall be carried out by the trader free of charge, without undue delay and no later than within 14 days from the date on which the trader is informed by the consumer of the consumer's decision to require a price reduction or the termination of the contract. Where the digital content was supplied on a carrier medium, the trader may, however, refrain from the reimbursement of payments after having submitted a request referred to in section 25, subsection 1 until the carrier medium has been returned to the trader.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:51] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158962: The trader shall carry out the reimbursement of payments received by the trader using the same means of payment as the consumer used in the initial transaction unless the consumer expressly agrees to some other arrangement. The consumer shall not incur any costs as a result of the reimbursement of payments.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:52]
PARAGRAPH_158963: Section 27 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:52]
PARAGRAPH_158964: Modification of digital content or service

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:52]
PARAGRAPH_158965: In the case of the supply of digital content or a digital service over a period of time, the trader may modify the digital content or service beyond what is necessary to keep the digital content or service in conformity if:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:52]
PARAGRAPH_158966: 1) the trader's right to unilaterally modify the digital content or service for a valid reason specified in the contract has been agreed in the contract;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:52]
PARAGRAPH_158967: 2) the modification is made without additional cost to the consumer; and

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:52]
PARAGRAPH_158968: 3) the consumer is informed in a clear and comprehensible manner of the modification.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:52] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158969: If the modification referred to in subsection 1 negatively impacts the consumer's access to or use of the digital content or service, the consumer shall be informed in good time on a durable medium of the features and time of the modification and of the right under subsection 3 to terminate the contract or of the possibility to maintain the digital content or service without such a modification. The information has been provided on a durable medium when it has been provided personally on paper or electronically in a manner which allows the unchanged storage and reproduction of the information by the recipient.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:52] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158970: If the modification of the digital content or service negatively impacts the consumer's access to or use of the digital content or service, the consumer has the right to terminate the contract free of charge within 30 days from the receipt of the information on the modification or of the time when the digital content or service has been modified by the trader, whichever is the later. The right to terminate the contract does not, however, exist if the negative impact of the modification is minor. The right to terminate the contract does not exist, either, when the trader has enabled the consumer to maintain without additional cost the digital content or service without the modification, and the digital content or digital service remains in conformity with the requirements of this chapter.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:52]
PARAGRAPH_158971: If the consumer terminates the contract under subsection 3, the provisions of sections 24-26 apply to the termination.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:52]
PARAGRAPH_158972: Section 28 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:52]
PARAGRAPH_158973: Limitation of loss or damage and adjustment of damages

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:53] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_158974: The consumer shall take reasonable measures to limit their loss or damage. Should they fail to comply with this, they themselves shall suffer the corresponding share of the loss or damage.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:53]
PARAGRAPH_158975: Damages payable on the basis of a breach of contract may be adjusted if they are disproportionate taking account of the cause of the breach of contract, the consumer's possible contribution to the loss or damage, the price of the digital content or service, the possibilities of the party causing the loss or damage to anticipate and prevent the occurrence of the loss or damage, as well as any other circumstances.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:53]
PARAGRAPH_158976: Section 29 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:53]
PARAGRAPH_158977: Statute of limitations on claims for compensation

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:53]
PARAGRAPH_158978: Provisions on the limitation period for the consumer's claim for compensation are laid down in the Act on the Statute of Limitations on Debt.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:53]
PARAGRAPH_158979: Chapter 6 (1211/2013) Off-premises selling and distance selling

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:53]
PARAGRAPH_158980: Section 1 (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:53]
PARAGRAPH_158981: Scope of application

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:53]
PARAGRAPH_158982: This chapter lays down provisions on the off-premises selling and distance selling of consumer goods and services.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:53]
PARAGRAPH_158983: Section 2 (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:53]
PARAGRAPH_158984: Limitations of scope of application

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:53]
PARAGRAPH_158985: The provisions of this chapter do not apply to:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:53]
PARAGRAPH_158986: 1) a contract for a financial service or instrument;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:53]
PARAGRAPH_158987: 2) a contract for the sale or rental of immovable property or for any other right in immovable property;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:53]
PARAGRAPH_158988: 3) a contract under the scope of application of the Housing Transactions Act;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:53]
PARAGRAPH_158989: 4) a contract for the assignment of a right of occupancy referred to in the Right-of-Occupancy Housing Act;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:53]
PARAGRAPH_158990: 5) a residential lease agreement referred to in the Act on Residential Leases;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_158991: 6) a contract under the scope of application of chapter 10;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_158992: Paragraph 7 was repealed by Act 902/2017.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_158993: 8) a contract for a service under the scope of application of the Lotteries Act;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_158994: 9) a contract concluded by means of automated vending machines or automated commercial premises;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_158995: 10) a contract concluded with a telecommunications operator through the use of a public payphone;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_158996: 11) a contract concerning individual deliveries of foodstuffs or other daily consumer goods to the consumer's residence or workplace using a regularly operating distribution system.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_158997: Section 3 (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_158998: Certain limitations of scope of application in off-premises selling

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_158999: The provisions of this chapter on off-premises selling do not apply if the price of the consumer good or service is lower than EUR 30. However, the provisions of this chapter do apply where multiple consumer goods or services the total price of which is a minimum of EUR 30 are sold at the same time, or if the contract concerns the continuous or recurring delivery of goods or services.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_159000: When providing a service in a place where the trader arrives at the consumer's express request, the provisions of this chapter on off-premises selling also do not apply to:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_159001: 1) a contract concerning social services;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:54] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159002: 2) a contract concerning health services provided for a consumer by a health professional to assess, maintain or restore the health of the consumer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_159003: Section 4 (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_159004: Application of provisions to certain services

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_159005: Only section 12, subsections 2 and 3 as well as sections 12a and 25 apply to contracts concerning passenger transport services and to travel packages referred to in the Act on Travel Service Combinations. (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:55]
PARAGRAPH_159006: In the case of a single service provided over the telephone, the contract for which is concluded immediately upon the consumer establishing a connection with the service provider, section 12, subsections 2-4 and sections 13 and 14 do not apply.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:55]
PARAGRAPH_159007: In the case of a contract that concerns communications services referred to in the Act on Electronic Communications Services, section 12a does not apply. (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:55]
PARAGRAPH_159008: Section 5 (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:55]
PARAGRAPH_159009: Mandatory nature of provisions

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:55]
PARAGRAPH_159010: Any contractual term deviating from the provisions of this chapter to the detriment of the consumer is null and void unless otherwise provided below.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:55]
PARAGRAPH_159011: Section 6 (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:55]
PARAGRAPH_159012: Definitions relating to off-premises selling

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:55]
PARAGRAPH_159013: Off-premises contract means any contract concluded, or any contract concerning which an offer was made by the consumer, in the simultaneous physical presence of the parties in a place which is not the business premises of the trader. Off-premises contract also means any contract concluded:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:55]
PARAGRAPH_159014: 1) on the business premises of the trader or through any means of distance communication immediately after the consumer was personally and individually addressed in a place which is not the business premises of the trader; or

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:55]
PARAGRAPH_159015: 2) during an excursion organised by the trader with the aim or effect of promoting and selling consumer goods or services to the consumer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:55]
PARAGRAPH_159016: Business premises means:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:55]
PARAGRAPH_159017: 1) any immovable sales premises where the trader offers consumer goods or services on a permanent or seasonal basis;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:55]
PARAGRAPH_159018: 2) any movable sales premises where the trader offers consumer goods or services on a usual or seasonal basis.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:55]
PARAGRAPH_159019: Section 7 (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:55]
PARAGRAPH_159020: Definitions relating to distance selling

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:56]
PARAGRAPH_159021: Distance contract means any consumer goods or service contract concluded under an organised distance sales or service-provision scheme without the simultaneous physical presence of the parties and with the exclusive use of one or more means of distance communication.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:56]
PARAGRAPH_159022: Means of distance communication means telephone, post, television, information network or other means that can be used to conclude a contract without the simultaneous physical presence of the parties.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:56]
PARAGRAPH_159023: Section 8 (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:56]
PARAGRAPH_159024: Other definitions

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:56]
PARAGRAPH_159025: For the purposes of this chapter:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:56]
PARAGRAPH_159026: 1) ancillary contract means a contract for consumer goods or services, relating to an off-premises or distance contract, that are supplied by the trader or a third party on the basis of a contract or another arrangement between that third party and the trader;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:56]
PARAGRAPH_159027: 2) provision of information on a durable medium means the provision of information personally on paper or electronically in a way that allows the unchanged storage and replication of the information by the recipient;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:56]
PARAGRAPH_159028: 3) supply of digital content means the supply of data produced and supplied electronically in a digital form through downloading, streaming or any other corresponding manner; (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:56]
PARAGRAPH_159029: 4) online marketplace means a service which provides the consumer with the opportunity to conclude distance contracts with other traders than the provider of the online marketplace or with private persons and which uses a website, application or other software or its part; (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:56]
PARAGRAPH_159030: 5) provider of an online marketplace means any trader who provides an online marketplace to consumers; (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:56]
PARAGRAPH_159031: 6) ranking means the relative prominence given by the trader to consumer goods or services as presented, organised or communicated by the trader to the consumer. (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:56]
PARAGRAPH_159032: Section 9 (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:56]
PARAGRAPH_159033: Information to be provided prior to concluding contract

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:56] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159034: Before the conclusion of an off-premises or distance contract, the consumer shall be provided with the following information:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:57]
PARAGRAPH_159035: 1) the main characteristics of the consumer good or service, to the extent appropriate taking account of the consumer good or service and the means of communication used;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:57]
PARAGRAPH_159036: 2) the name of the trader;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:57]
PARAGRAPH_159037: 3) the geographical address of the trader in the state of establishment and, where the trader is acting as an agent or representative of another trader, the name and geographical address of the trader's principal;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:57]
PARAGRAPH_159038: 4) the telephone number and email address of the trader and, where necessary, the details of any other means of electronic communication allowing the consumer to contact the trader quickly and communicate with the trader efficiently and enabling the unchanged storage and replication of the correspondence with the trader by the consumer; (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:57]
PARAGRAPH_159039: 5) if different from the address referred to in paragraph 3, the geographical address of the place of business of the trader where the consumer can address any complaints and, where the trader is acting as an agent or representative of another trader, the same details of the trader's principal;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:57]
PARAGRAPH_159040: 6) the total price of the consumer good or service inclusive of taxes or, where the nature of the good or service is such that the exact price cannot reasonably be calculated in advance, the price determination criteria and, where necessary, the fact that the price was personalised on the basis of automated decision-making; (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:57]
PARAGRAPH_159041: 7) where necessary, any delivery and other charges not included in the total price for the consumer goods or services or, where these costs cannot reasonably be calculated in advance, the fact that such additional charges may be payable;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:57]
PARAGRAPH_159042: 8) the cost of using the means of distance communication for the conclusion of the contract where that cost is higher than the basic rate;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:57]
PARAGRAPH_159043: 9) the terms concerning payment, delivery and other performance of the contract and, where necessary, the customer complaint handling policy;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:57]
PARAGRAPH_159044: 10) where necessary, the conditions, time limits and procedures for exercising the right of withdrawal;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:58]
PARAGRAPH_159045: 11) where necessary, that the consumer will have to bear the cost of returning the goods in case of withdrawal from the contract by the consumer and, for distance selling, if the goods, by their nature, cannot normally be returned in the usual manner by post, the cost of returning the goods;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:58]
PARAGRAPH_159046: 12) that, if the consumer exercises the right of withdrawal after having made a request concerning the performance of the service referred to in section 15, subsection 1, the consumer is liable to pay the trader reasonable costs referred to in section 19, subsection 1;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:58]
PARAGRAPH_159047: 13) where necessary, the information that the consumer will not benefit from the right of withdrawal or the circumstances under which the consumer may lose the right of withdrawal;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:58]
PARAGRAPH_159048: 14) a reminder of the existence of a legal guarantee of conformity for goods as well as digital content and services; (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:58]
PARAGRAPH_159049: 15) where necessary, the existence and the conditions of customer assistance, other after-sales services and guarantees;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:58]
PARAGRAPH_159050: 16) the existence of codes of conduct and, where necessary, how copies of them can be obtained;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:58]
PARAGRAPH_159051: 17) where necessary, the duration of the contract or, where the contract is of indeterminate duration or is to be extended automatically, the conditions for terminating the contract;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:58]
PARAGRAPH_159052: 18) where necessary, the minimum duration of the consumer's obligations under the contract;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:58]
PARAGRAPH_159053: 19) where necessary, the existence and the conditions of financial guarantees that the trader requires from the consumer;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:58]
PARAGRAPH_159054: 20) where necessary, the functionality, including applicable technical protection measures, of a good with digital elements and of digital content or a digital service, and any compatibility and interoperability of such a consumer good or service that the trader is aware of or can reasonably be expected to be aware of; (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:58]
PARAGRAPH_159055: 21) the possibility and methods of referring a dispute to be considered by the Consumer Disputes Board or another equivalent body.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:59]
PARAGRAPH_159056: In an auction that can be attended by the consumer also in a manner other than through a means of distance communication, the information referred to in subsection 1, paragraphs 2-5 may be replaced by equivalent details of the auctioneer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:59] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159057: If the consumer has the right of withdrawal under the off-premises or distance contract, the consumer shall, in addition to the information referred to in subsection 1, paragraph 10, be provided with a withdrawal form. The information referred to in subsection 1, paragraphs 10-12 above may be provided in the instructions on withdrawal. Provisions on the format and contents of the withdrawal form and instructions are laid down by decree of the Ministry of Justice.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:59]
PARAGRAPH_159058: Section 9a (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:59]
PARAGRAPH_159059: Obligations of provider of online marketplace to provide information

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:59] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159060: If the contract is concluded on an online marketplace, the provider of the marketplace shall, before concluding the contract, provide the consumer with the following information in a manner that is clear, comprehensible and appropriate to the means of distance communication:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:59]
PARAGRAPH_159061: 1) the information referred to in chapter 2, section 8d, subsection 1;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:59]
PARAGRAPH_159062: 2) whether the third party offering the consumer goods or services is a trader or not, on the basis of the declaration of that third party, and where the third party is not a trader, that the rights arising from consumer protection law do not apply;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:59]
PARAGRAPH_159063: 3) where necessary, how the obligations related to the contract are shared between the third party offering the consumer good or service and the provider of the online marketplace.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:59]
PARAGRAPH_159064: Section 10 (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:59]
PARAGRAPH_159065: Certain other consumer information

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:59] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159066: In telemarketing, the trader shall immediately at the beginning of a telephone call disclose the trader's name and, where necessary, the name of the person on whose behalf the trader is acting, as well as the commercial purpose of the call.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:59] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159067: Trading websites shall indicate clearly at or before the beginning of the ordering process whether any delivery restrictions apply and which means of payment are accepted.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:59]
PARAGRAPH_159068: Section 11 (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:59]
PARAGRAPH_159069: Provision of prior information in off-premises selling

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:60] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159070: In off-premises selling, the information referred to in section 9 as well as the withdrawal form and the instructions on withdrawal shall be given to the consumer clearly and comprehensibly on paper or, if the consumer agrees, on another durable medium.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:60]
PARAGRAPH_159071: Section 12 (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:60]
PARAGRAPH_159072: Provision of prior information in distance selling

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:60] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159073: In distance selling, the information referred to in section 9 as well as the withdrawal form and the instructions on withdrawal shall be given or made available to the consumer in a clear and comprehensible manner appropriate to the means of distance communication. If the information, form or instructions are provided on a durable medium, they shall be legible.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:60] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159074: If a contract to be concluded by electronic means places the consumer under an obligation to pay, the consumer shall be made aware in a clear manner, and directly before the consumer places their order, of the matters referred to in section 9, subsection 1, paragraphs 1, 6, 7, 17 and 18. The trader shall also ensure that the consumer explicitly acknowledges that the order implies an obligation to pay.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:60] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159075: If the trader has not complied with the provision of subsection 2 on the consumer's explicit acknowledgment, the consumer is not bound by the contract. Should the consumer wish to rely on the contract being non-binding, the consumer shall notify this to the trader no later than one year from the conclusion of the contract. If the contract lapses when the consumer has relied on it being non-binding, the trader shall without delay and no later than 30 days from having received the notification reimburse any payments received by the trader and reimburse to the consumer the cost of returning the goods.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:60] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159076: If the contract is concluded through a means of distance communication which allows limited space or time to display the information, the trader shall provide, on that particular means prior to the conclusion of such a contract, at least the information referred to in section 9, subsection 1, paragraphs 1, 2, 6, 7, 10 and 17.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:60]
PARAGRAPH_159077: Section 12a (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:60]
PARAGRAPH_159078: Conclusion of contract in telemarketing

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:60] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159079: If the trader offers the consumer a consumer good or service over the telephone and the consumer in that context states their willingness to conclude a contract with the trader, the trader shall after the telephone conversation provide the consumer with the trader's offer on paper or on another durable medium. If the consumer has not after the telephone conversation accepted on a durable medium the offer provided by the trader on a durable medium, the consumer is not bound

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:61] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159080: by the contract and the consumer shall therefore not be required to make payments, return or retain the consumer goods or carry out any other measure.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:61] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159081: The consumer shall be notified in conjunction with being provided with an offer in accordance with subsection 1 that, should the consumer not accept the offer on a durable medium, the consumer is not bound by the contract and is not obliged to pay for the consumer good or service or to return or retain it. The burden of proof of the consumer having been provided with the offer in a manner required by subsection 1 and the consumer having received the notification referred to in this subsection is on the trader.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:61]
PARAGRAPH_159082: The provisions of this section do not apply if the consumer has at their own initiative contacted the trader or if the trader has contacted the consumer at the consumer's explicit request.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:61]
PARAGRAPH_159083: Section 13 (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:61]
PARAGRAPH_159084: Confirmation of information

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:61] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159085: In off-premises selling, the trader shall provide the consumer with a copy of the confirmation of the contract or a copy of the signed contract on paper or, if the consumer agrees, on another durable medium.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:61] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159086: In distance selling, the trader shall provide the consumer with a confirmation of the concluded contract within a reasonable period of time after the conclusion of the distance contract and at the latest by the time of delivery of the goods or before the performance of the service begins. The confirmation shall be provided on a durable medium and shall include all of the information referred to in section 9 as well as the withdrawal form and the instructions on withdrawal unless the trader has already provided that information to the consumer on a durable medium before that.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:61] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159087: If the electronic supply of digital content begins before the end of the withdrawal period, the confirmation shall also include the consumer's prior express consent and acknowledgement that they will lose the right of withdrawal referred to in section 15, subsection 2. (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:61]
PARAGRAPH_159088: Section 13a (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:61]
PARAGRAPH_159089: Burden of proof of obligations concerning provision of information having been fulfilled

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:61]
PARAGRAPH_159090: The burden of proof of the trader having fulfilled the trader's obligations in accordance with sections 9, 9a, 10-12 and 13 is on the trader.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:61]
PARAGRAPH_159091: Section 14 (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:62]
PARAGRAPH_159092: Right of withdrawal

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:62]
PARAGRAPH_159093: The consumer has the right to withdraw from an off-premises or distance contract by informing the trader about this by means of submitting the withdrawal form or any other unequivocal statement no later than 14 days from the conclusion of the service contract or the contract for the electronic supply of digital content, in the case of a sales contract from the receipt of the goods or the last instalment of goods or, in the case of the regular delivery of goods, from the receipt of the first instalment of goods.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:62]
PARAGRAPH_159094: If the trader has failed to provide the consumer with the information referred to in section 9, subsection 1, paragraph 10, the withdrawal period expires in 12 months from the expiry of the time limit referred to in subsection 1 of this section or, if the trader corrects this shortcoming during that period, in 14 days from the date on which the consumer received the information.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:62] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159095: If the trader provides the consumer with the option to submit a notification of withdrawal via the trader's website, the trader shall communicate to the consumer without delay on a durable medium an acknowledgement of receipt of the withdrawal notification.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:62]
PARAGRAPH_159096: The burden of proof of the withdrawal from the contract having been carried out as required by this section is on the consumer. (572/2020)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:62]
PARAGRAPH_159097: Section 15 (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:62]
PARAGRAPH_159098: Performance of service before expiry of withdrawal period

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:62] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159099: If the contract places the consumer under an obligation to pay, the performance of a service other than a service relating to digital content may begin before the expiry of any withdrawal period provided that the consumer has explicitly requested this and acknowledged that the consumer will no longer have the right of withdrawal once the contract has been fully performed by the trader. In off-premises selling, the request shall be made on a durable medium.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:62] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159100: If the contract places the consumer under an obligation to pay, the electronic supply of digital content may begin before the expiry of any withdrawal period if the consumer has given their prior express consent to the beginning of the performance of the contract during the withdrawal period and acknowledged that the consumer loses their right of withdrawal when giving their consent. The trader shall provide a confirmation of the consumer's prior express consent and acknowledgement in the manner referred to in section 13.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:62]
PARAGRAPH_159101: Section 16 (1211/2013) Limitations of right of withdrawal

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:63]
PARAGRAPH_159102: Unless otherwise agreed, the consumer does not have the right of withdrawal laid down in section 14 if:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:63]
PARAGRAPH_159103: 1) the service has been fully performed and, if the contract places the consumer under an obligation to pay, the performance of the contract began when the consumer made a request referred to in section 15, subsection 1 and acknowledged that the consumer will lose their right of withdrawal once the contract has been fully performed by the trader; (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:63]
PARAGRAPH_159104: 2) the price of the consumer good or service is dependent on fluctuations in the financial market which cannot be controlled by the trader and which may occur within the withdrawal period;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:63]
PARAGRAPH_159105: 3) the contract concerns goods made to the customer's specifications or clearly personalised;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:63]
PARAGRAPH_159106: 4) the contract concerns goods which are liable to deteriorate or expire rapidly or which are, after delivery, according to their nature, inseparably mixed with other items;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:63]
PARAGRAPH_159107: 5) the supply of sealed goods which are not suitable for return due to health protection or hygiene reasons and have been unsealed;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:63]
PARAGRAPH_159108: 6) the contract concerns the supply of alcoholic beverages, the price of which has been agreed upon at the time of the conclusion of the contract, the delivery of which can only take place after 30 days and the actual value of which is dependent on fluctuations in the market which cannot be controlled by the trader;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:63]
PARAGRAPH_159109: 7) the contract concerns urgent repairs or maintenance in a place that the trader is specifically requested by the customer to visit;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:63]
PARAGRAPH_159110: 8) the supply of sealed audio or sealed video recordings or sealed computer software which has been unsealed;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:63]
PARAGRAPH_159111: 9) the supply of a single copy of a newspaper, periodical or magazine;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:63]
PARAGRAPH_159112: 10) the contract has been concluded in an auction that can be attended by the consumer also in a manner other than through a means of distance communication;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:63]
PARAGRAPH_159113: 11) the contract concerns the provision of accommodation other than for residential purposes, transport of goods, car rental services, catering or services related to leisure activities and the contract provides for a specific date or period of performance; (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:64]
PARAGRAPH_159114: 12) the electronic supply of digital content has begun and, if the contract places the consumer under the obligation to pay:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:64]
PARAGRAPH_159115: a) the consumer has given their prior express consent to the beginning of the performance of the contract during the withdrawal period;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:64]
PARAGRAPH_159116: b) the consumer has acknowledged that they will not have the right of withdrawal in such a case; and

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:64]
PARAGRAPH_159117: c) the trader has provided the consumer with the confirmation referred to in section 13. (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:64]
PARAGRAPH_159118: Notwithstanding the provisions of subsection 1, paragraph 7, the consumer has the right of withdrawal laid down in section 14 where, on the occasion of a visit referred to in the said paragraph, the trader provides services in addition to those specifically requested by the consumer or goods other than replacement parts necessarily used in carrying out the maintenance or in making the repairs. (572/2020)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:64]
PARAGRAPH_159119: Notwithstanding the provisions of subsection 1, paragraphs 1 and 3, the consumer has the right of withdrawal in accordance with section 14 in off-premises selling if the contract was concluded in conjunction with a home visit made by the trader without the consumer's request. (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:64]
PARAGRAPH_159120: Section 17 (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:64]
PARAGRAPH_159121: Return of goods and reimbursement of payments

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:64] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159122: If the consumer withdraws from an off-premises or distance contract, the consumer shall return the goods received by them without delay and no later than 14 days after having submitted the withdrawal notification unless the trader has undertaken to collect the goods. The consumer shall bear the direct costs of returning the goods unless the trader has undertaken to bear them. Provisions on the consumer's right not to pay the costs referred to above if the trader has failed to inform about them are laid down in section 24, subsection 1.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:64] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159123: If in the case of off-premises selling the goods have been delivered to the consumer's home in conjunction with the conclusion of the contract, the trader shall, however, at the trader's own expense collect the goods if, by their nature, those goods cannot normally be returned by post.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:64] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159124: The trader shall, without delay and no later than 14 days after the trader's receipt of the withdrawal notification, reimburse the payments received from the consumer except for any supplementary costs arising from a type of delivery, other than the least expensive type of

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:65]
PARAGRAPH_159125: standard delivery offered by the trader, that the consumer has opted for. Unless the trader is obliged to collect the goods themselves, the trader may, however, withhold the reimbursement until the trader has received the goods back or until the consumer has supplied evidence of having sent back the goods.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:65] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159126: The trader shall carry out the reimbursement of payments received by the trader using the same means of payment as the consumer used in the initial transaction unless the consumer has expressly consented to another arrangement. The consumer shall not incur any costs as a result of such reimbursement.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:65]
PARAGRAPH_159127: Section 17a (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:65]
PARAGRAPH_159128: Parties' rights and obligations when consumer withdraws from contract for digital content or service

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:65] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159129: If the consumer withdraws from the contract, the consumer shall refrain from using the digital content or service and from making it available to third parties. When the contract is withdrawn from, the trader has the right to make the digital content or service inaccessible by the consumer, disable the user account of the consumer or in another manner prevent the use of the digital content or service unless otherwise provided in subsection 3.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:65] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159130: The trader shall refrain from using the content which was provided or created by the consumer through the use of the digital content or service unless:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:65]
PARAGRAPH_159131: 1) the content has no utility outside the context of the digital content or service supplied by the trader;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:65]
PARAGRAPH_159132: 2) the content only relates to the consumer's activity when using the digital content or service supplied by the trader;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:65]
PARAGRAPH_159133: 3) the content has been aggregated with other data by the trader and cannot be disaggregated or only with disproportionate efforts; or

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:65]
PARAGRAPH_159134: 4) the content has been generated jointly by the consumer and other consumers, and other consumers are able to continue to make use of the content.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:65] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159135: In cases other than those referred to in subsection 2, paragraphs 1-3, the trader shall, at the request of the consumer, make available to the consumer any content which was provided or created by the consumer when using the digital content or service supplied by the trader. The

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:66] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159136: request shall be carried out free of charge within a reasonable time and in a commonly used and machine-readable format.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:66]
PARAGRAPH_159137: The provisions of subsections 2 and 3 do not apply to personal data. Provisions on the use of personal data are laid down in Regulation (EU) 2016/679 of the European Parliament and of the Council on the protection of natural persons with regard to the processing of personal data and on the free movement of such data, and repealing Directive 95/46/EC (General Data Protection Regulation).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:66]
PARAGRAPH_159138: Section 18 (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:66]
PARAGRAPH_159139: Liability for goods received

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:66] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159140: If the consumer has received the goods, the consumer shall keep the goods essentially unchanged and unreduced until the consumer has decided to keep the goods.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:66] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159141: If the consumer, however, withdraws from the contract after having taken the goods into use, the consumer is liable for any reduction in the value of the goods. The goods are not deemed as having been taken into use if the consumer has handled the goods only as necessary to establish the nature, characteristics and functioning of the goods.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:66]
PARAGRAPH_159142: The consumer is not liable for any reduction in value if the trader has failed to provide the consumer with the information on the right of withdrawal referred to in section 9, subsection 1, paragraph 10.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:66]
PARAGRAPH_159143: Section 19 (572/2020)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:66]
PARAGRAPH_159144: Compensation for service performed before withdrawal

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:66] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159145: If the performance of a service other than a service concerning digital content has begun before the expiry of the withdrawal period, the consumer shall, in the event of withdrawal, pay the trader reasonable compensation for the performance carried out to perform the contract until the submission of the withdrawal notification. The amount of compensation is calculated on the basis of the total price under the contract. If the total price is unreasonable, the amount to be paid is calculated on the basis of the market value of the service performed for the consumer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:66]
PARAGRAPH_159146: The consumer is not, however, liable to pay for a service performed in full or in part during the withdrawal period if the trader has failed to provide the consumer with the information referred to in section 9, subsection 1, paragraph 10 or 12 or if the trader has begun the performance of the contract without the consumer's express request referred to in section 15, subsection 1.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:66]
PARAGRAPH_159147: Section 20 (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:67]
PARAGRAPH_159148: Retention and return of goods in certain cases

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:67] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159149: If the trader is obliged in off-premises selling to collect the goods from the consumer, the consumer shall in the event of withdrawal keep the received goods accessible by the trader in the place where the trader delivered the goods or from where the trader can collect the goods without difficulty. The consumer shall notify the trader of the place from where the goods can be collected.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:67]
PARAGRAPH_159150: The consumer's liability for the retention of the goods on behalf of the trader ends in two months from the receipt of the goods. The consumer may keep the goods without remuneration if the trader fails to collect the goods within the said period of time unless this is manifestly unreasonable for the trader.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:67]
PARAGRAPH_159151: Section 21 (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:67]
PARAGRAPH_159152: Termination of credit agreement or insurance contract

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:67]
PARAGRAPH_159153: If the consumer withdraws from an off-premises or distance contract, any ancillary credit agreement or insurance contract is automatically terminated.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:67] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159154: In the event of the termination of an ancillary credit agreement or insurance contract, the creditor or insurance provider shall without delay and no later than 30 days from having been informed of the termination of the contract reimburse any payments received by the creditor or insurance provider from the consumer. Provisions on the insurance provider's right to require payment for any insurance cover received by the policyholder before the termination of an ancillary insurance policy are laid down in section 45 of the Insurance Contracts Act (543/1994).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:67]
PARAGRAPH_159155: Section 22 (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:67]
PARAGRAPH_159156: Termination of other ancillary contracts

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:67] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159157: If the consumer withdraws from an off-premises or distance contract, any ancillary contract other than those referred to in section 21 is automatically terminated. The consumer shall not incur any costs as a result of the termination other than any costs payable under sections 17-19.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:67]
PARAGRAPH_159158: Section 23 (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:67]
PARAGRAPH_159159: Interest for late payment

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:67]
PARAGRAPH_159160: Provisions on the consumer's right to interest for late payment in situations where a trader or a creditor or insurance provider liable for the reimbursement of a price or other payment has failed to reimburse a payment made by the consumer within the period of time laid down in section 12, 17 or 21 are laid down in the Interest Act.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:67]
PARAGRAPH_159161: Section 24 (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:68]
PARAGRAPH_159162: Consequences of violations of certain provisions of the chapter

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:68]
PARAGRAPH_159163: If the trader has failed to provide the consumer before the conclusion of the contract the information concerning additional costs or other costs referred to in section 9, subsection 1, paragraphs 6, 7 or 11, the consumer is not obliged to pay them.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:68]
PARAGRAPH_159164: In the case of a contract for electronically supplied digital content, the consumer is not obliged to pay for a service performed in full or in part if:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:68]
PARAGRAPH_159165: 1) the supply of the digital content began during the withdrawal period without the consumer's prior express consent or acknowledgement referred to in section 15, subsection 2; (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:68]
PARAGRAPH_159166: 2) the consumer has not acknowledged that the consumer loses their right of withdrawal when giving their consent; or

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:68]
PARAGRAPH_159167: 3) the trader has failed to provide the consumer with the confirmation referred to in section 13.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:68] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159168: The consumer is not bound by the contract if the trader in off-premises selling has failed to provide the consumer with the information referred to in section 9, subsection 1, paragraph 13 in the manner laid down in section 11 before the conclusion of the contract. Should the consumer wish to rely on the contract being non-binding, the consumer shall notify this to the trader within 12 months from the conclusion of the contract. If the contract lapses when the consumer has relied on it being non-binding, the trader shall without delay and no later than 30 days from having received the notification reimburse any payments received by the trader and reimburse to the consumer the cost of returning the goods or other performance. (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:68]
PARAGRAPH_159169: Section 25 (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:68]
PARAGRAPH_159170: Consequences of violations of provisions of the chapter

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:68]
PARAGRAPH_159171: In addition to the provisions of this chapter on consequences, where necessary for consumer protection, a prohibitory injunction may be imposed on a trader that violates the provisions of this chapter to refrain from continuing or repeating such a practice or a comparable practice. Provisions on the imposition of a prohibitory injunction and its enforcement by a notice of a conditional fine are laid down in chapters 2 and 3.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:68]
PARAGRAPH_159172: Provisions on penalty fees imposed for violations of provisions of section 9 of this chapter and provisions laid down under it as well as of provisions of section 9a; sections 10-12, sections 12a and 13; and section 14, subsections 1 and 2; section 17, subsections 2-4; and section 17a,

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:69]
PARAGRAPH_159173: subsections 1-3 of this chapter are laid down in the Act on Certain Powers of the Consumer Protection Authorities. (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:69]
PARAGRAPH_159174: Chapter 6a (29/2005)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:69]
PARAGRAPH_159175: Distance selling of financial services and financial instruments

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:69]
PARAGRAPH_159176: Section 1 (29/2005)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:69]
PARAGRAPH_159177: Scope of application

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:69]
PARAGRAPH_159178: This chapter lays down provisions on distance selling where a trader offers to a consumer:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:69]
PARAGRAPH_159179: 1) deposit or customer accounts;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:69]
PARAGRAPH_159180: 2) payment transfer services;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:69]
PARAGRAPH_159181: 3) credits or credit intermediation;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:69]
PARAGRAPH_159182: 4) insurance policies or insurance intermediation;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:69]
PARAGRAPH_159183: 5) units in funds or other securities to which the Securities Markets Act applies;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:69]
PARAGRAPH_159184: 6) securities brokerage or other investment services;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:69]
PARAGRAPH_159185: 7) investment advice; or

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:69]
PARAGRAPH_159186: 8) other financial services or financial instruments.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:69]
PARAGRAPH_159187: The provisions of this chapter below on financial services also apply to financial instruments.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:69]
PARAGRAPH_159188: Section 2 (29/2005)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:69]
PARAGRAPH_159189: Limitations of application of provisions in certain cases

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:69]
PARAGRAPH_159190: If a distance contract between a trader and a consumer concerns the continuous or recurrent supply of financial services of the same nature, the provisions of this chapter do not apply to individual service performances based on the contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:69]
PARAGRAPH_159191: If the same parties conclude recurrent contracts on financial services of the same kind, sections 5-11 of this chapter only apply to the first contract. However, sections 5-11 also apply if a period longer than one year has elapsed since the previous contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:70]
PARAGRAPH_159192: Section 11b does not apply to consumer credit falling within the scope of application of chapter 7 or 7a of this Act. (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:70]
PARAGRAPH_159193: Section 3 (29/2005)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:70]
PARAGRAPH_159194: Mandatory nature of provisions

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:70]
PARAGRAPH_159195: Any contractual term deviating from the provisions of this chapter to the detriment of the consumer is null and void.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:70]
PARAGRAPH_159196: Section 4 (29/2005)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:70]
PARAGRAPH_159197: Definitions

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:70]
PARAGRAPH_159198: Distance selling means in this chapter the supply of a financial service to a consumer by using a distance provision scheme organised by the trader where the conclusion of the contract and the pre-contract marketing make exclusive use of one or more means of distance communication.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:70]
PARAGRAPH_159199: Distance provision scheme means a method of marketing or selling organised in such a way that its primary aim can be deemed to be the conclusion of contracts using a means of distance communication.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:70]
PARAGRAPH_159200: Means of distance communication means telephone, post, television, information network or other means that can be used to conclude a contract without the simultaneous physical presence of the parties.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:70]
PARAGRAPH_159201: Section 5 (29/2005)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:70]
PARAGRAPH_159202: Obligation to provide information before concluding contract

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:70] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159203: Besides other legal provisions elsewhere on obligations to provide information, the consumer shall be provided in good time before concluding the contract the information referred to in sections 6-9 on the trader, the financial service to be supplied, the distance contract and the legal remedies. The information shall be provided in a way that is appropriate to the means of distance communication, that is clear and comprehensible and that clearly discloses the commercial purpose of the information.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:70]
PARAGRAPH_159204: Section 6 (29/2005)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:70]
PARAGRAPH_159205: Prior information on trader

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:70] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159206: At least the following information shall be provided on the trader:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:70]
PARAGRAPH_159207: 1) name and principal activity, geographical address in the state of establishment and the geographical address of the place of business managing customer relations;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_159208: 2) any branch or other representative in the consumer's state of residence and the geographical address of the place of business of the branch or representative where customer relations are managed;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_159209: 3) the name of the intermediary or agent acting on behalf of the trader, the geographical address of the place of business managing customer relations, and information on the representation nature of the activity, when the consumer deals with an intermediary or agent;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_159210: 4) any trade register or other similar public register in which the trader is entered, and the trader's business identity code or other similar identifier in the register;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_159211: 5) where the activity is subject to authorisation or registration, the particulars of the relevant supervisory authority.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_159212: Section 7 (29/2005)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_159213: Prior information on financial service

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:71] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159214: At least the following information shall be provided on the financial service:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_159215: 1) a description of the main characteristics of the financial service;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_159216: 2) the total amount of fees, charges and other costs, including taxes, to be paid by the consumer or, when an exact amount cannot be indicated, the criteria for determining the costs;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_159217: 3) notice of any possible capital gains tax, asset transfer tax and similar taxes or public charges relating to the acquisition of financial services of which the trader is aware and which the consumer may have to pay in addition to the costs payable to the trader referred to in paragraph 2;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_159218: 4) the arrangements for payment of costs and performance of contract;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_159219: 5) any costs arising from using the means of distance communication, if a charge additional to the basic rate is charged;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_159220: 6) where necessary, notice indicating that the financial service may involve the risk of losing the funds invested or any other special risk and that past performance concerning price or value is no guarantee of future performance;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_159221: 7) any limitations of the period for which the information provided is valid.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:72]
PARAGRAPH_159222: Section 8 (29/2005)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:72]
PARAGRAPH_159223: Prior information on distance contract

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:72] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159224: At least the following information shall be provided on the distance contract:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:72]
PARAGRAPH_159225: 1) the existence of a right of withdrawal, or the absence of the right under the law;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:72]
PARAGRAPH_159226: 2) the withdrawal period, the amount of compensation that may be required from the consumer due to withdrawal, or the criteria for determining the compensation if an exact amount of compensation cannot be indicated, as well as other conditions and instructions concerning the exercise of the right of withdrawal;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:72]
PARAGRAPH_159227: 3) the minimum duration of the contract if the contract concerns financial services to be performed permanently or recurrently;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:72]
PARAGRAPH_159228: 4) any right the parties may have to cancel, terminate or perform the contract early under the law or by virtue of a contractual term as well as the consequences of such measures;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:72]
PARAGRAPH_159229: 5) the state on the basis of whose legislation the prior information is provided;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:72]
PARAGRAPH_159230: 6) any contractual terms concerning law applicable to the contract and the competent court;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:72]
PARAGRAPH_159231: 7) in which language or languages the consumer can receive the prior information and contractual terms in the manner laid down in section 11 and in which language or languages the trader undertakes to communicate during the duration of the contractual relationship.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:72]
PARAGRAPH_159232: Section 9 (29/2005)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:72]
PARAGRAPH_159233: Prior information on legal remedies

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:72] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159234: At least the following information shall be provided on legal remedies:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:72]
PARAGRAPH_159235: 1) whether or not there is an out-of-court redress mechanism and, if so, the methods for having access to it;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:72]
PARAGRAPH_159236: 2) the existence of guarantee funds or other compensation arrangements providing consumer protection not based on European Community legislation.

PARAGRAPH_159237: Section 10 (29/2005)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:72]
PARAGRAPH_159238: Prior information in telemarketing

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:73] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159239: In telemarketing, the name of the trader, the name of the person discussing with the consumer and the commercial purpose of the call shall be disclosed to the consumer immediately at the beginning of the conversation.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:73] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159240: The trader need not provide all of the information specified in sections 6-9 over the telephone if the consumer gives their express consent to this. In such a case, the consumer shall be informed that other information is available to them on request and of what nature this information is. The following information shall, however, always be provided:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:73]
PARAGRAPH_159241: 1) the relationship with the trader of the person discussing with the consumer, such as whether they are employed by the trader or an agent, other representative or intermediary acting on behalf of the trader;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:73]
PARAGRAPH_159242: 2) a description of the main characteristics of the financial service;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:73]
PARAGRAPH_159243: 3) the total amount of fees, charges and other costs, including taxes, to be paid for the performance of the financial service by the consumer or, when an exact amount cannot be indicated, the criteria for determining the costs;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:73]
PARAGRAPH_159244: 4) notice of any possible capital gains tax, asset transfer tax and similar taxes or public charges relating to the acquisition of financial services of which the trader is aware and which the consumer may have to pay in addition to the costs payable to the trader referred to in paragraph 3;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:73]
PARAGRAPH_159245: 5) the existence of a right of withdrawal, or the absence of the right under the law;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:73]
PARAGRAPH_159246: 6) the withdrawal period, the amount of compensation that may be required from the consumer due to withdrawal or the criteria for determining the compensation if an exact amount cannot be indicated, as well as other conditions and instructions concerning the exercise of the right of withdrawal.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:73]
PARAGRAPH_159247: Section 11 (29/2005)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:73]
PARAGRAPH_159248: Communication of prior information and contractual terms on paper or on another durable medium

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:73] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159249: The prior information and contractual terms shall be communicated to the consumer in good time before the conclusion of the contract personally on paper or electronically in a way which allows its unchanged storage and reproduction by the consumer. The same applies to information that the

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:74] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159250: trader must under other legislation provide to the consumer before the conclusion of a contract for the financial service.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:74] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159251: If the contract is concluded at the consumer's request using a means of distance communication which does not enable providing the information and the contractual terms on a durable medium as referred to in subsection 1 before the conclusion of the contract, the information and the contractual terms shall be provided on a durable medium without delay after the conclusion of the contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:74]
PARAGRAPH_159252: During the contractual relationship, the consumer has the right, at their request, to receive the contractual terms on paper.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:74]
PARAGRAPH_159253: Section 11a (851/2016)
