PARAGRAPH_159254: Housing credits

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:74]
PARAGRAPH_159255: The creditor is deemed to have fulfilled the information provision obligations laid down in sections 5-9 in the manner required by section 11 if the creditor has delivered the European Standardised Information Sheet form (ESIS form) concerning the housing credit offered to the consumer before the conclusion of the contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:74]
PARAGRAPH_159256: Section 11b (693/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:74]
PARAGRAPH_159257: Conclusion of contract in telemarketing

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:74] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159258: If the trader offers the consumer a financial service over the telephone and the consumer in that context states their willingness to conclude a contract with the trader, the trader shall after the telephone conversation provide the consumer with the trader's offer on paper or on another durable medium. If the consumer has not after the telephone conversation accepted on a durable medium the offer provided by the trader on a durable medium, the consumer is not bound by the contract and the consumer shall therefore not be required to make payments, return or retain a performance or carry out any other measure.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:74] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159259: Should the consumer wish to rely on the contract being non-binding, the consumer shall notify this to the trader within one year from the conclusion of the contract. If the contract lapses when the consumer has relied on it being non-binding, the trader shall without delay and no later than 30 days from having received the notification reimburse any payments received by the trader.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:74] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159260: The consumer shall be notified in conjunction with being provided with an offer in accordance with subsection 1 that, should the consumer not accept the offer on a durable medium, the consumer is not bound by the contract if they inform the trader of this within one year from the conclusion of

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:75]
PARAGRAPH_159261: the contract. The burden of proof of the consumer having been provided with the offer in a manner required by subsection 1 and the consumer having received the notification referred to in this subsection is on the trader.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:75]
PARAGRAPH_159262: The provisions of this section do not apply if the consumer has at their own initiative contacted the trader or if the trader has contacted the consumer at the consumer's explicit request.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:75]
PARAGRAPH_159263: Section 12 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:75]
PARAGRAPH_159264: Right of withdrawal

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:75]
PARAGRAPH_159265: The consumer has the right to withdraw from the contract by informing the trader about this within 14 days from the conclusion of the contract or from a later date on which the consumer received the prior information and the contractual terms on a durable medium.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:75]
PARAGRAPH_159266: The provisions of subsection 1 and sections 14-16 on withdrawal from the contract do not apply to consumer credits and insurance policies. The provisions of section 13, subsection 1 also do not apply to consumer credits. Provisions on the consumer's right to withdraw from a consumer credit agreement and repay a consumer credit early are laid down in chapters 7 and 7a. Provisions on the policyholder's right to withdraw from or terminate an insurance contract are laid down in the Insurance Contracts Act. (851/2016)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:75]
PARAGRAPH_159267: Notwithstanding the provisions of subsection 2, the provisions of subsection 1, sections 14-16 and section 13, subsection 1 apply to credits granted by pawnbrokers.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:75]
PARAGRAPH_159268: Section 13 (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:75]
PARAGRAPH_159269: Termination of ancillary contract

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:75]
PARAGRAPH_159270: Any ancillary contract related to a contract for the distance selling of a financial service is automatically terminated when the consumer withdraws from the principal contract if the ancillary service is also provided by the same trader. An ancillary contract is also terminated if a third party provides the ancillary service on the basis of a contract or other arrangement between the trader that concluded the principal contract and the third party.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:75]
PARAGRAPH_159271: Section 14 (29/2005)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:75]
PARAGRAPH_159272: Limitations of right of withdrawal

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:75]
PARAGRAPH_159273: The consumer does not have the right of withdrawal laid down in section 12 if:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:75]
PARAGRAPH_159274: 1) the price or value of the financial service or a related financial instrument is dependent on fluctuations in the financial market which cannot be controlled by the trader; or

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:76]
PARAGRAPH_159275: 2) the contracting parties have already fulfilled their contractual obligations in full at the consumer's explicit request.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:76]
PARAGRAPH_159276: Section 15 (29/2005)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:76]
PARAGRAPH_159277: Compensation for service performed before withdrawal

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:76] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159278: If the consumer withdraws from the contract, the consumer may be required to compensate only for such a service that the trader has actually performed under the contract before the withdrawal. The compensation shall not exceed the amount obtained by comparing the service performed with the services referred to in the contract in full.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:76]
PARAGRAPH_159279: If the trader has not disclosed the compensation or the criteria for its determination in advance or if the trader has begun the performance of the contract without the consumer's explicit request, the consumer need not compensate for the service performed.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:76]
PARAGRAPH_159280: Section 16 (29/2005)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:76]
PARAGRAPH_159281: Reimbursement of payments and assets

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:76] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159282: The consumer shall without delay and no later than 30 days from the date of dispatch of the withdrawal notification reimburse to the trader all of the payments and other assets received by the consumer under the contract on pain of the withdrawal otherwise lapsing. The consumer may, however, refrain from fulfilling their own reimbursement obligation until the trader fulfils their own equivalent obligation.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:76] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159283: The trader shall without delay and no later than 30 days from the date of receipt of the withdrawal notification reimburse to the consumer all of the payments and assets received by the trader from the consumer under the contract. Any compensation that the trader under section 15 has the right to receive from the consumer for a service performed before the withdrawal from the contract may be deducted from the payments and assets reimbursed.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:76]
PARAGRAPH_159284: Section 17 (29/2005)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:76]
PARAGRAPH_159285: Limitation of choice-of-law clauses

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:76] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159286: A choice-of-law clause under which the law of a non-European Economic Area state is applied to the contract shall not prevail over provisions in force in a Member State of the European Economic Area applied, in the absence of a choice-of-law clause, to the distance selling of financial services if these provisions provide consumers with more effective protection than the law applied under the choice-of-law clause.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:76]

PARAGRAPH_159293: Chapter 7 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:77]
PARAGRAPH_159294: Consumer credits

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:77]
PARAGRAPH_159295: General provisions

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:77]
PARAGRAPH_159296: Section 1 (851/2016)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:77]
PARAGRAPH_159297: Scope of application

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:77]
PARAGRAPH_159298: This chapter lays down provisions on consumer credits. Consumer credit means credit that a trader (creditor) under an agreement grants or promises to grant to a consumer in the form of a loan, deferred payment or other similar financial accommodation.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:77]
PARAGRAPH_159299: In the application of the provisions of this chapter, a lease or other such agreement under which the goods are handed over to the possession of the consumer, and under the terms of which the cash price of the goods and costs of credit will be paid during the lease period or the consumer can otherwise become the owner of the goods at the end of the agreement, is comparable to consumer credit.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:77] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159300: In the application of the provisions of this chapter other than the provisions of section 16a, credit that a party other than the creditor grants or promises to grant to a consumer in the form of a loan, deferred payment or another equivalent financial arrangement is also comparable to consumer credit if a trader intermediates the credit to the consumer. In such cases, the trader intermediating the credit to the consumer shall ensure that the said provisions are complied with in the credit relationship.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:78]
PARAGRAPH_159301: In the application of the provisions of section 40, an identifier that provides access to an account or other financial service or financial instrument is comparable to an identifier providing access to the credit. In such cases, the provisions concerning the creditor apply to the trader that has concluded the agreement concerning the identifier with the consumer. (899/2017)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:78]
PARAGRAPH_159302: The provisions of this chapter do not apply to:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:78]
PARAGRAPH_159303: 1) consumer credit for which no interest or other payments are charged;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:78]
PARAGRAPH_159304: 2) credit based on an agreement under which the consumer has the right to pay the price of goods or services supplied on a continuing basis by means of instalments over the duration of the agreement;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:78]
PARAGRAPH_159305: 3) credit granted by a pawnbroker;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:78]
PARAGRAPH_159306: 4) credit granted under the Act on Social Lending (1133/2002);

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:78]
PARAGRAPH_159307: 5) housing credit or consumer credit secured by a residence falling under the scope of application of chapter 7a, unless otherwise provided in the said chapter.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:78]
PARAGRAPH_159308: Section 2 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:78]
PARAGRAPH_159309: Limitations of application of provisions in credits linked to current accounts and in payment arrangement agreements

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:78] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159310: The provisions of section 3; section 8, subsection 1, paragraphs 3-5 and subsection 3; sections 9- 12; section 13, subsection 2, paragraph 2; sections 17, 18 and 20-23; section 24, subsections 2- 4; sections 25, 27-32, 36-39 and 47 do not apply to consumer credit linked to a current account under the contractual terms of which the credit period is a maximum of three months or the credit must be repaid on demand.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:78]
PARAGRAPH_159311: Only sections 5-7, 47, 50 and 51 apply to consumer credit granted by the creditor by allowing the overrunning of a current account or credit limit without this having been expressly agreed between the parties.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:78]
PARAGRAPH_159312: Sections 9-12 do not apply to a payment arrangement agreement, concluded due to a consumer's payment difficulties, the terms of which are not less favourable to the consumer than the initial credit agreement.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:78]
PARAGRAPH_159313: Section 3 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:79]
PARAGRAPH_159314: Limitations of application of provisions in certain other cases

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:79]
PARAGRAPH_159315: Sections 9-11, section 13, subsection 2, paragraph 4 as well as sections 14 and 17 of this chapter do not apply to consumer credit where the credit period is a maximum of three months, no interest is charged and the other costs of credit payable expressed as an annual percentage rate of charge do not exceed the amount of interest referred to in section 4, subsection 1 of the Interest Act. Sections 14 and 17 apply, however, to running account credit. (207/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:79]
PARAGRAPH_159317: Sections 18 and 39 of this chapter apply only to goods-or-services-linked credit and sections 36-38 only to goods-or-services-linked credit granted for the acquisition of goods.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:79]
PARAGRAPH_159318: Section 17a of this chapter does not apply to hire purchase agreements where the subject of the sale is a means of transport, including any accessories, to be registered in the transport register referred to in the Act on Transport Services (320/2017). The said section applies, however, if the consumer has the right under the agreement to also withdraw funds. (596/2019)

PARAGRAPH_159325: Section 5 (851/2016)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:79]
PARAGRAPH_159326: Mandatory nature of provisions

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:79]
PARAGRAPH_159327: Any contractual term deviating from the provisions of this chapter to the detriment of the consumer is null and void. Any contractual term of a credit agreement referred to in section 1, subsection 3 that deviates from the provisions of the chapter to the detriment of the consumer is also null and void.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:80]
PARAGRAPH_159328: Section 6 (596/2019)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:80]
PARAGRAPH_159329: Costs of credit and interest

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:80]
PARAGRAPH_159330: Costs of credit mean in this chapter the total amount of interest, costs and other charges which the consumer has to pay and which are known to the creditor; costs of credit also include the costs of any insurance policies and other ancillary services linked to the credit agreement if the conclusion of the contract for the ancillary service is a condition for the credit being granted on the terms and conditions marketed.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:80]
PARAGRAPH_159331: Costs of credit do not include:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:80]
PARAGRAPH_159332: 1) costs payable for the account used for servicing the credit if opening the account is voluntary and the costs are broken down in the agreement;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:80]
PARAGRAPH_159333: 2) payments to be made by the consumer due to any breach of agreement;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:80]
PARAGRAPH_159334: 3) notarial costs.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:80]
PARAGRAPH_159335: Annual percentage rate of charge means in this chapter the percentage rate of interest obtained by calculating the costs of credit as an annual rate of interest for the amount of credit, taking account of repayments. Provisions on the method of calculation of the annual percentage rate of charge and the assumptions used in the calculation are laid down by decree of the Ministry of Justice.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:80]
PARAGRAPH_159336: Borrowing rate means in this chapter the interest rate expressed as a fixed or variable percentage applied on an annual basis to the amount of credit drawn.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:80]
PARAGRAPH_159337: Section 7 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:80]
PARAGRAPH_159338: Other definitions

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:80]
PARAGRAPH_159339: For the purposes of this chapter:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:80]
PARAGRAPH_159340: 1) running account credit means consumer credit available continuously to the consumer up to the credit limit agreed without a separate credit decision by the creditor;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:80]
PARAGRAPH_159341: 2) one-off credit means consumer credit other than running account credit;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:80]
PARAGRAPH_159342: 3) goods-or-services-linked credit means consumer credit granted for the acquisition of consumer goods or services that is granted by the seller or the service provider by themselves or by

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:81]
PARAGRAPH_159343: another trader under a contract or another consumer credit provision arrangement concluded with the seller or service provider;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:81]
PARAGRAPH_159344: 4) staff means persons employed by, or otherwise acting on behalf of, the creditor or credit intermediary who take part in the granting or intermediating of consumer credit and persons under whose direct management and supervision the former persons act; (851/2016)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:81]
PARAGRAPH_159345: 5) hire purchase means the sale of goods under an agreement for which the price is paid in repayment instalments, one or more of which fall due after the delivery of the goods to the consumer (buyer), and where the trader (seller) has retained the right to either repossess the goods, if the buyer fails to fulfil an obligation of the buyer under the agreement, or the right of ownership to the goods until the price has been paid in full or at least a specific part of also those repayment instalments falling due after the delivery of the goods has been paid;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:81]
PARAGRAPH_159346: 6) credit intermediary means a trader other than a creditor who presents or offers credit agreements to consumers or otherwise assists consumers in the conclusion of credit agreements or concludes credit agreements with consumers on behalf of a creditor;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:81]
PARAGRAPH_159347: 7) provision of information on a durable medium means the provision of information to a consumer personally on paper or electronically in a way that allows the unchanged storage and replication of the information by the consumer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:81]
PARAGRAPH_159348: Obligations to provide information

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:81]
PARAGRAPH_159349: Section 8 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:81]
PARAGRAPH_159350: Information to be provided when advertising consumer credit

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:81] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159351: Advertising of consumer credit shall indicate the annual percentage rate of charge if the advertising indicates the borrowing rate or another figure relating to any cost payable for the credit or any other information concerning the terms of the credit agreement. In addition, in such cases the advertising shall indicate the following information:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:81]
PARAGRAPH_159352: 1) the borrowing rate and other costs of credit;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:81]
PARAGRAPH_159353: 2) the amount of credit or the credit limit;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:81]
PARAGRAPH_159354: 3) the duration of the credit agreement;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:82]
PARAGRAPH_159355: 4) the cash price of the good or service and any deposit in the case of credit advertised to finance the purchase of a specific good or service;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:82]
PARAGRAPH_159356: 5) the total amount credit and costs of credit and the number of repayment instalments.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:82] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159357: The annual percentage rate of charge and the other information specified in subsection 1 shall be given in advertising in a clear, concise and prominent way and correspond to the terms and conditions of credit normally offered by the creditor. (851/2016)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:82] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159358: Where it is a compulsory condition, in order to obtain the credit on the terms and conditions advertised, that the consumer concludes a contract concerning insurance or another ancillary service and the costs of that ancillary service cannot be determined in advance, such a condition shall be stated together with the annual percentage rate of charge.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:82]
PARAGRAPH_159359: Subsection 4 was temporarily in force from 1 July 2020 to 31 December 2020 under Act 512/2020 and from 1 January 2021 to 30 September 2021 under Act 1194/2020. (1194/2020)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:82]
PARAGRAPH_159360: Section 8a (1194/2020)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:82]
PARAGRAPH_159361: Section 8a was temporarily in force from 1 January 2021 to 30 September 2021 under Act 1194/2020.

PARAGRAPH_159362: Section 9 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:82]
PARAGRAPH_159363: Information preliminary to conclusion of credit agreement

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:82] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159364: Besides other legal provisions elsewhere concerning obligations to provide information, the creditor and the credit intermediary shall in good time before the conclusion of the credit agreement provide the consumer with the information on the following by means of the Standard European Consumer Credit Information Form:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:82]
PARAGRAPH_159365: 1) the creditor;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:82]
PARAGRAPH_159366: 2) the credit offered, the costs of credit and the repayment of the credit;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:82]
PARAGRAPH_159367: 3) the good or service financed by the credit;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:82]
PARAGRAPH_159368: 4) the consequences of a breach of agreement;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:82]
PARAGRAPH_159369: 5) the consumer's legal rights.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:83]
PARAGRAPH_159370: In the case of goods-or-service-linked one-off credits of less than EUR 100, the information may also be provided on another durable medium instead of the form. Further provisions on the prior information and the form are laid down by Government Decree. (851/2016)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:83] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159371: If the credit agreement intends to refer to a benchmark referred to in Article 3(1)(3) of Regulation (EU) 2016/1011 of the European Parliament and of the Council on indices used as benchmarks in financial instruments and financial contracts or to measure the performance of investment funds and amending Directives 2008/48/EC and 2014/17/EU and Regulation (EU) No 596/2014, the creditor and the credit intermediary shall, in addition, provide the consumer on a separate document with information on the benchmark and the name of its administrator as well as on the possible impacts of the use of the benchmark on the consumer. (1096/2017)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:83]
PARAGRAPH_159372: Section 10 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:83]
PARAGRAPH_159373: Prior information in telemarketing

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:83] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159374: In addition to the provisions laid down in chapter 6a, section 10, subsection 1 and subsection 2, paragraphs 1 and 3-6 on prior information to be provided in telemarketing, the creditor and the credit intermediary shall in telemarketing provide the consumer with the information on the credit offered, the costs of credit and the repayment of the credit as well as the goods or service to be financed. Further provisions on the information to be provided are laid down by Government Decree.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:83]
PARAGRAPH_159375: Section 11 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:83]
PARAGRAPH_159376: Certain other provisions on obligation to provide prior information

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:83] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159377: If the agreement is concluded at the consumer's request over the telephone or using another means of distance communication which does not enable supplying the Standard European Consumer Credit Information Form on a durable medium before the conclusion of the agreement, the form shall be provided on a durable medium without delay after the conclusion of the agreement. In the case of goods-or-services-linked one-off credits of less than EUR 100, the prior information shall be provided on the form or on another durable medium without delay after the conclusion of the agreement if the agreement is concluded at the consumer's request over the telephone or using another means of distance communication which does not enable providing the prior information before the conclusion of the agreement. (851/2016)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:83] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159378: The consumer shall, in addition, be supplied on request and free of charge, with a copy of the draft credit agreement. Provisions on the supply of the contractual terms in distance selling are laid down in chapter 6a.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:84]

PARAGRAPH_159380: Exception concerning credit intermediaries acting in ancillary capacity

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:84]
PARAGRAPH_159381: The provisions of sections 9-11 on the credit intermediary's obligation to provide the consumer with information do not apply to sellers or service providers acting as credit intermediaries in an ancillary capacity alongside their primary activity.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:84]
PARAGRAPH_159382: Creditor's obligation to act responsibly

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:84]
PARAGRAPH_159383: Section 13 (207/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:84]
PARAGRAPH_159384: Good lending practice

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:84] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159385: The creditor shall act responsibly in granting credit.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:84]
PARAGRAPH_159386: It is required in particular that the creditor:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:84]
PARAGRAPH_159387: 1) does not market the credit in a way that is likely to clearly reduce the consumer's capacity to carefully consider whether or not to obtain the credit;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:84]
PARAGRAPH_159388: 2) does not use the granting of the credit as the primary marketing method when marketing other consumer goods or services;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:84]
PARAGRAPH_159389: 3) does not use, when marketing or granting the credit, or in any other transactions relating to the credit relationship, premium text message services or other corresponding message services;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:84] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159390: 4) provides the consumer, before the conclusion of the agreement, with adequate and clear explanations for the consumer to assess whether the credit and any ancillary services offered are adapted to the consumer's needs and their financial situation, and information on whether the consumer may terminate the contract for the ancillary service separately and which consequences to the consumer arise from this; (851/2016)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:84]
PARAGRAPH_159391: 5) provides the consumer in late payment situations with information and advice on how to prevent the emergence or worsening of payment difficulties, and takes a responsible stance towards payment arrangements.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:84]
PARAGRAPH_159392: The provisions of subsection 1 and subsection 2, paragraphs 1-4 also apply to credit intermediaries. The provisions of subsection 2, paragraph 4 do not, however, apply to sellers or service providers acting as ancillary credit intermediaries alongside their primary activity.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:85] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159393: The staff remuneration systems of creditors and credit intermediaries shall not be such that they prevent conduct in credit granting, credit intermediation and provision of advisory services from being in compliance with the requirements of subsections 1 and 2. (851/2016)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:85]
PARAGRAPH_159394: Section 13a (851/2016)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:85]
PARAGRAPH_159395: Prohibition of tying practice

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:85] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159396: It shall not be a condition for a credit offer that the consumer concludes an agreement for another financial service or another service or financial instrument that the creditor itself or another trader offers on the basis of a contract or another arrangement concluded with the creditor.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:85]

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:85]

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:85]
PARAGRAPH_159399: Section 14 (207/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:85] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159400: Obligation to assess consumer's creditworthiness

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:85] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159401: Before concluding a credit agreement, the creditor shall assess the prospect of the consumer to meet their obligations under the credit agreement ( consumer's creditworthiness). The assessment shall be carried out on the basis of sufficient credit register and other information on the consumer's income and other financial and economic circumstances. (740/2022)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:85]
PARAGRAPH_159402: Subsection 1 as amended by Act 740/2022 enters into force on 1 April 2024. Previous form of wording:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:85] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159403: Before concluding a credit agreement, the creditor shall assess the prospect of the consumer to meet their obligations under the credit agreement ( consumer's creditworthiness). The assessment shall be carried out on the basis of sufficient information on the consumer's income and other financial and economic circumstances.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:85] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159404: If the parties subsequently agree on an increase in the amount of credit or the credit limit, the creditor shall ensure the up-to-dateness of the information on the consumer and, if the amount of credit or the credit limit is to be increased significantly, the consumer's creditworthiness shall be reassessed before agreeing on the increase.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:85]
PARAGRAPH_159405: Section 15 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:85]
PARAGRAPH_159406: Verification of credit applicant's identity

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:85] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159407: The creditor shall before concluding a consumer credit agreement carefully verify the identity of the person applying for the credit. If the identity is verified electronically, the creditor shall use an

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:86]
PARAGRAPH_159408: identification method that meets the requirements laid down in section 8 of the Act on Strong Electronic Identification and Electronic Trust Services (617/2009). (899/2017)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:86]
PARAGRAPH_159409: If the creditor has previously identified the consumer in a manner referred to in subsection 1, the consumer's identity may also be verified using a personal identifier created for them after the initial identification.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:86]
PARAGRAPH_159410: Provisions on customer due diligence are, in addition, laid down in the Act on Preventing Money Laundering and Terrorist Financing (444/2017). (457/2017)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:86]
PARAGRAPH_159411: Section 16 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:86]
PARAGRAPH_159412: Obligation to retain information concerning identification

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:86] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159413: Unless otherwise provided in the Act on Detecting and Preventing Money Laundering and Terrorist Financing (503/2008), the creditor shall retain the information on the basis of which the consumer applying for the credit was identified for five years from the date on which the credit became due for repayment in full. In the event of a dispute concerning a credit agreement, the information on identification shall, however, be retained until the matter has been settled or resolved.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:86]
PARAGRAPH_159414: Section 16a (851/2016)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:86]
PARAGRAPH_159415: Granting of credit

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:86] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159416: The creditor shall determine the principles employed by the creditor in granting consumer credits.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:86]
PARAGRAPH_159417: The creditor may grant credit to the consumer only if the result of the assessment of the consumer's creditworthiness indicates that the obligations resulting from the credit agreement are likely to be met in the manner required under the credit agreement.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:86]
PARAGRAPH_159418: Conclusion of credit agreement and release of funds

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:86]
PARAGRAPH_159419: Section 17 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:86]
PARAGRAPH_159420: Conclusion of credit agreement

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:86] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159421: A consumer credit agreement shall be concluded in writing and the consumer shall be provided with a copy of the agreement. The agreement may also be concluded electronically in a way that allows the unchanged storage and replication of the agreement by the consumer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:86] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159422: A consumer credit agreement shall specify:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:86]
PARAGRAPH_159423: 1) information on the parties to the credit agreement;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:87]
PARAGRAPH_159424: 2) information on the matters referred to in section 9;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:87]
PARAGRAPH_159425: 3) any other contractual terms;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:87]
PARAGRAPH_159426: 4) information on the conditions for the exercise of the right of withdrawal;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:87]
PARAGRAPH_159427: 5) information on the termination and other cessation of the agreement;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:87]
PARAGRAPH_159428: 6) information on the legal remedies and supervisory authority.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:87] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159429: Further provisions on the information to be specified in the agreement are laid down by Government Decree. No interest or payments that have not been agreed upon under the agreement referred to in subsection 1 shall be charged to the consumer on the basis of the credit relationship.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:87]
PARAGRAPH_159430: Section 17a (596/2019)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:87]
PARAGRAPH_159431: Maximum amount of costs of credit

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:87] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159432: The borrowing rate charged for the credit drawn shall not be agreed to be greater than 20 per cent.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:87] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159433: If the consumer under the agreement must pay costs of credit other than those referred to in subsection 1, the amount of these per day shall not exceed 0.01 per cent of the amount of credit or the credit limit for the duration of the credit agreement.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:87] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159434: Notwithstanding the provisions of subsection 2, the maximum amount of other costs of credit may be agreed as being EUR 5, provided that the credit period under the agreement is at least 30 days. The costs payable by the consumer on the basis of subsection 2 shall not exceed EUR 150 per year, and the costs of credit may not be charged to the consumer in advance for a period longer than one year.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:87]
PARAGRAPH_159435: If the creditor or the credit intermediary violates a provision of this section, the consumer is not obliged to pay any interest paid on the borrowing rate or any other costs of credit at all.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:87]
PARAGRAPH_159436: The provisions of subsections 2-4 do not apply to insurance premiums regarded as costs of credit if the purpose of the insurance is to safeguard the value of a surety provided for the credit.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:87]
PARAGRAPH_159437: If the consumer repays the credit early, the provisions of sections 27 and 28 apply notwithstanding the provisions of subsections 2 and 3 of this section. If the credit is called in, the provisions of section 35 apply notwithstanding the provisions of subsections 2 and 3.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:88]
PARAGRAPH_159438: Section 17b (596/2019)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:88]
PARAGRAPH_159439: Costs charged for extending repayment period

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:88]
PARAGRAPH_159440: The consumer may be charged a maximum of EUR 5 for the extension of the repayment period before the amount falls due, provided that the repayment period is extended by a minimum of 14 days. The consumer may not, however, be charged a total amount of costs exceeding EUR 20 per year for such measures.

Such an instrument shall not be accepted from a person living in a shared household with the consumer, either.

PARAGRAPH_159450: If consumer credit is applied for and granted between 23.00 and 7.00, the funds granted under the credit agreement may be paid to the consumer only after 7.00. The provisions of this section do not apply to increases of the credit limit of running account credit.

PARAGRAPH_159451: Withdrawal from credit agreement

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:88]
PARAGRAPH_159452: Section 20 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:88]
PARAGRAPH_159453: Right of withdrawal

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:88]
PARAGRAPH_159454: The consumer has the right to withdraw from a consumer credit agreement by informing the creditor of this on a durable medium within 14 days from the conclusion of the agreement or from

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:89]
PARAGRAPH_159455: a later date on which the consumer received a copy of the credit agreement containing the information in accordance with section 17 or 45 on paper or electronically.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:89] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159456: If the consumer withdraws from the agreement, the consumer may be required to pay as compensation the borrowing rate for the period during which the credit was available to the consumer. If the creditor has made payments to the authorities due to the conclusion of the credit agreement and such payments are not reimbursed in the event of withdrawal, the creditor has the right to compensation from the consumer also for such payments. Interest or payments shall not, however, be required if the payment obligation or the amount of interest or payments or, if the amount of interest cannot be disclosed in advance, the criteria for its determination, have not been disclosed to the consumer in advance.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:89] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159457: The consumer shall without delay and no later than 30 days from the date of dispatch of the withdrawal notification reimburse to the trader all of the funds received by the consumer under the credit agreement and make the payments under subsection 2 on pain of the withdrawal otherwise lapsing. The consumer may, however, refrain from fulfilling their own payment obligation until the trader fulfils their own corresponding obligation.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:89]
PARAGRAPH_159458: Section 21 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:89]
PARAGRAPH_159460: Any ancillary contract related to a consumer credit agreement is not binding on the consumer when the consumer withdraws from the credit agreement if the ancillary service is also provided by the creditor. An ancillary contract is also not binding on the consumer if a third party provides the ancillary service on the basis of a contract or other arrangement between the creditor and the third party.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:89] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159461: If the consumer wishes to keep the ancillary contract in force regardless of the withdrawal from the credit agreement, the consumer shall notify the creditor of this within 30 days from the dispatch of the withdrawal notification.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:89]

PARAGRAPH_159466: 2) a credit agreement involving a total amount of less than EUR 200 or more than EUR 75,000;

PARAGRAPH_159467: 3) a credit agreement that is linked to a current account and under the terms of which the credit period is a maximum of one month;

PARAGRAPH_159476: Consumer's right to receive amortisation table on request

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:91] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159477: If the credit agreement has been concluded for a fixed period and the amortisation of the debt under its terms takes place in instalments, the creditor shall, during the contractual relationship, provide the consumer free of charge with an amortisation table whenever the consumer requests it. (851/2016)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:91] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159478: The amortisation table shall indicate the payments owing and the periods and conditions relating to the payment of such amounts. There shall be a breakdown of each repayment separately showing capital amortisation, the interest payable and any other payments. If the amount of interest or any other payments may be changed under the terms of the credit agreement, the table shall, in addition, indicate that the data contained in the table will remain valid only until such time as such changes are made in accordance with the credit agreement.

PARAGRAPH_159479: Section 24 (851/2016)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:91]
PARAGRAPH_159480: Changes in interest and payments

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:91] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159481: The interest payable on the credit by the consumer may during the credit agreement change only in accordance with changes in the reference rate specified in the agreement and provided that this has been agreed upon in the consumer credit agreement. The reference rate applied shall be publicly available and based on factors independent of any unilateral control of the creditor. The creditor shall retain the information on the level of the reference rate for five years from the date on which the credit became due for repayment in full. In the event of a dispute concerning a credit agreement, the information shall, however, be retained until the matter has been settled or resolved.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:91] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159482: Any changes in the interest rate shall be carried out equally and in a manner that is non- discriminatory to consumers, and the consumer shall be informed of them on a durable medium before a change enters into force. The information on the change shall state the amount of the payments to be made after the change in the interest rate and, if the number or frequency of the payments changes, up-to-date particulars of these.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:91]
PARAGRAPH_159483: If the information on a new reference rate is made publicly available by appropriate means and the information is also kept available on the premises of the creditor, the information referred to in subsection 2 may, notwithstanding the provisions of the said subsection, be given to the consumer periodically as agreed under the agreement but, however, at least once a year.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:91] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159484: Payments charged under the credit agreement may only be changed on grounds specified in the agreement. An increase in payment shall not be greater than the actual increase in costs incurred by the creditor on the basis of which the payment is charged under the credit agreement. The

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:92]
PARAGRAPH_159485: provisions of subsections 2 and 3 on changes in the interest rate apply to provision of information on changes in payments.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:92]
PARAGRAPH_159498: The consumer has the right to repay the consumer credit or part of it before the credit becomes due for repayment.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:92] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159499: In the event of the early repayment by the consumer of the credit in full or in part, the part of the costs of credit relating to the credit period that will remain unused shall be deducted from the outstanding payments to the creditor. The creditor may, however, charge in full any actual costs arising from measures relating to the setting up of the credit in question specified in the credit agreement.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:92]
PARAGRAPH_159500: Section 28 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:92]
PARAGRAPH_159501: Creditor's right to compensation for early repayment

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:93]
PARAGRAPH_159502: The creditor has the right to compensation from the consumer in the event of their early repayment of the credit in full or in part if the borrowing rate is not linked to a reference rate (fixed interest rate).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:93] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159503: The amount of the compensation shall not exceed one per cent of the amount of credit repaid or, if the period of time between the early repayment and the agreed termination of the credit agreement does not exceed one year, half a per cent of the amount of credit repaid. The amount of compensation charged shall, however, be no more than the amount of interest for the period of time between the early repayment and the agreed termination of the credit agreement.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:93]
PARAGRAPH_159504: However, there is no right to compensation if:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:93]
PARAGRAPH_159505: 1) the amount of credit repaid early over the past year is no more than EUR 10,000;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:93]
PARAGRAPH_159506: 2) the repayment takes place under a credit protection insurance; or

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:93]
PARAGRAPH_159507: 3) the credit repaid is based on a credit agreement linked to a current account.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:93]

PARAGRAPH_159510: Section 30 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:93]
PARAGRAPH_159511: Termination of agreement for running account credit

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:93] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159512: The consumer may at any time during the contractual relationship terminate an agreement for running account credit with immediate effect unless the parties have agreed upon a period of notice. A period of notice to be observed by the consumer shall not exceed one month.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:93] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159513: The creditor may terminate an agreement for running account credit under the terms agreed in the credit agreement. A period of notice to be observed by the creditor shall not be shorter than two months. A notice of termination shall be delivered to the consumer on a durable medium.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:93]
PARAGRAPH_159514: Section 31 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:93]
PARAGRAPH_159515: Costs charged for termination

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:93] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159516: The creditor shall not charge the consumer for any payments for the termination of an agreement for running account credit. The consumer shall pay any costs charged regularly for the credit agreement only to the extent that these relate to the period before the termination takes effect. If the consumer has paid such costs in advance, the creditor shall reimburse them to the extent that they relate to the period after the termination takes effect.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:94]
PARAGRAPH_159517: Section 32 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:94]
PARAGRAPH_159518: Creditor's right to terminate consumer's right to use running account credit

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:94] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159519: The terms of the credit agreement may stipulate that the creditor has, on the grounds specified in the agreement, the right to terminate the consumer's right to use the running account credit. The grounds shall be in compliance with good lending practice.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:94] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159520: The creditor shall inform the consumer of the termination of the right of use and the reasons for it on a durable medium in advance. If the termination of the right of use with immediate effect is necessary to prevent or restrict abuse, loss or damage, the notification may be given without delay after the termination.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:94] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159521: The notification shall not be given if giving it is prohibited elsewhere by law.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:94]
PARAGRAPH_159522: Section 33 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:94]
PARAGRAPH_159523: Consequences of consumer's breach of agreement

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:94]
PARAGRAPH_159524: If the agreement gives the creditor the right, due to the consumer's late payment or other breach of agreement, to require the payment of an instalment that is otherwise not yet due for payment, repossess the goods sold or effect some other specific consequence, the creditor may rely on the said right if the payment is delayed by at least a month and still remains unpaid. In the case of one-off credit, a further condition is that the delayed amount is at least ten per cent or, if the amount includes more than one instalment, at least five per cent of the original amount of credit or covers the entire remaining amount outstanding to the creditor. In the case of credit granted to finance the purchase of a specific good or service, the percentages referred to above are calculated from the credit price. The creditor may rely on the right referred to above also if the consumer's other breach of agreement is material.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:94]
PARAGRAPH_159525: Notwithstanding the provisions of subsection 1 on the amount of the late payment, the creditor has the right to effect the agreed consequence if the payment is delayed by at least six months and it still remains to a material extent unpaid.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:94]
PARAGRAPH_159526: Section 34 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:94]
PARAGRAPH_159527: Social force majeure

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:94]
PARAGRAPH_159528: The creditor does not have the right to effect a consequence referred to in section 33 in the case of late payment where the late payment is due to the consumer's ill health, unemployment or some other equivalent reason not attributable to the consumer, except where this would be manifestly unreasonable for the creditor taking account of the duration of the delay and other circumstances.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:95]
PARAGRAPH_159529: Section 35 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:95]
PARAGRAPH_159530: Calling in

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:95] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159531: If the creditor requires the repayment of instalments that are otherwise not yet due for payment, when calculating the amount payable to the creditor the part of the costs of credit relating to the credit period that will remain unused shall be deducted from these repayment instalments. The creditor may, however, charge in full any actual costs arising from measures relating to the setting up of the credit in question specified in the credit agreement. Any credit period remaining unused is regarded as beginning from the date on which the instalments called in are due.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:95]
PARAGRAPH_159532: Credit repayment instalments called in may fall due no earlier than four weeks or, if the consumer has previously been reminded of the delay or other breach of agreement, no earlier than two weeks from the date on which the notification of the instalments being called in was lodged or sent to the consumer. If the consumer during this period of time repays the delayed amount or remedies the other breach of agreement, the calling in lapses.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:95]
PARAGRAPH_159533: Section 36 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:95]
PARAGRAPH_159534: Settlement of accounts

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:95] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159535: If the creditor repossesses the goods, a settlement of accounts shall be carried out between the creditor and the consumer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:95] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159536: In the settlement of accounts, the value of the goods when repossessed shall be credited to the consumer. The value is determined on the basis of what the seller can be assumed to have once the goods have been sold in an appropriate manner and, where necessary, reasonably refurbished. When determining the value, account shall be taken of the cash price specified in the agreement and the duration for which the goods have been in the possession of the consumer and how the goods have been looked after.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:95] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159537: The following shall be credited to the creditor:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:95]
PARAGRAPH_159538: 1) the unpaid part of the credit less the deduction in accordance with section 35, subsection 1;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:95]
PARAGRAPH_159539: 2) the interest on the instalments due for payment;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:95]
PARAGRAPH_159540: 3) the necessary costs and payments incurred by the creditor in repossessing the goods which the creditor has to pay to repossess the goods;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:95]
PARAGRAPH_159541: 4) the amounts outstanding to the creditor for refurbishing or maintenance of the goods if the creditor for this reason has the right to retain the goods.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:96]
PARAGRAPH_159542: If the value of the goods in the settlement of accounts is found to exceed the amount to be credited to the creditor, the creditor does not have the right to repossess the goods unless the creditor pays the difference to the consumer or, if the goods have been valued by an enforcement officer, deposits the said difference with the enforcement officer. If the value of the goods is lower than the amount that is to be credited to the creditor, the creditor does not, in addition to the goods, have the right to require any amount greater than the difference of these.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:96] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159543: If the consumer pays the amount, that under subsection 3 shall be credited to the creditor, in a single payment, the consumer may keep the goods. If the consumer has not exercised this right and the creditor has repossessed the goods, the buyer has the right to redeem the goods within 14 days by paying to the creditor the amount at which the goods were valued when repossessed as well as any difference that the creditor has the right to require under subsection 4.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:96]
PARAGRAPH_159544: Section 37 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:96]
PARAGRAPH_159545: Executive assistance

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:96]
PARAGRAPH_159546: The creditor has the right to seek executive assistance from an enforcement officer to repossess the goods if a hire purchase agreement was concluded as referred to in section 17, subsection 1 and it specifies:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:96]
PARAGRAPH_159547: 1) information on the parties to the credit agreement;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:96]
PARAGRAPH_159548: 2) information on the goods to be financed by the credit and their delivery;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:96]
PARAGRAPH_159549: 3) information on the credit offered, the costs of credit and the repayment of the credit;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:96]
PARAGRAPH_159550: 4) any other contractual terms;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:96]
PARAGRAPH_159551: 5) information on the conditions for the exercise of the right of withdrawal;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:96]
PARAGRAPH_159552: 6) information on the termination and other cessation of the agreement;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:96]
PARAGRAPH_159553: 7) information on the consequences of any breach of contract;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:96]
PARAGRAPH_159554: 8) information on the consumer's legal rights;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:96]
PARAGRAPH_159555: 9) information on the competent authority for settlement of accounts concerning hire purchase;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:96]
PARAGRAPH_159556: 10) information on the legal remedies and supervisory authority.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:97] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159557: Executive assistance shall be sought from an enforcement officer of the location of the goods or the place of residence or domicile of the consumer. The application shall be made in writing and state the amounts required by the creditor in accordance with section 36, subsection 3. The application shall be accompanied by the hire purchase agreement.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:97] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159558: Executive assistance shall be provided only if it is evident that the creditor has the right under sections 33 and 34 to repossess the goods. Executive assistance shall not be provided if the consumer can show that it is probable that the consumer, due to the seller's breach of contract, has the right to refrain from paying the price of the goods.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:97]
PARAGRAPH_159559: Further provisions on the information to be specified in the hire purchase agreement are laid down by Government Decree.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:97]
PARAGRAPH_159560: Section 38 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:97]
PARAGRAPH_159561: Certain other provisions on hire purchase

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:97]
PARAGRAPH_159562: The provisions of section 9, subsection 3 and sections 11-19 of the Hire-Purchase Act (91/1966) apply, in addition, to settlement of accounts, provision of executive assistance and distraint of goods based on receivables other than those based on hire purchase.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:97]
PARAGRAPH_159563: Liability provisions

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:97]
PARAGRAPH_159564: Section 39 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:97]
PARAGRAPH_159565: Joint liability of creditor and seller or service provider

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:97]
PARAGRAPH_159566: A consumer who has the right to withhold payment or receive a payment reimbursement, damages or another monetary payment from a seller or service provider due to their breach of contract also has this right in relation to the creditor that financed the sale or service. The creditor is not, however, liable to pay to the consumer any amount exceeding the payments the creditor has received from the consumer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:97]
PARAGRAPH_159567: If the seller repossesses the goods or if the sales contract is otherwise terminated under an agreement between the seller and the consumer, the consumer may rely on a settlement of accounts or termination of sales contract also against the creditor that finances the sale. The consumer does not, however, have such a right if:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:97]
PARAGRAPH_159568: 1) the creditor has in advance informed the consumer in a clear manner that the seller does not have the right of repossession or another right to exercise control over the contract and, if the

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:98] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159569: subject of the sale is goods that must under law be registered, the creditor is entered in the register as the owner; or

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:98]
PARAGRAPH_159570: 2) the creditor is otherwise able to demonstrate that the consumer was aware of the restriction of the seller's rights.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:98]
PARAGRAPH_159571: Section 40 (899/2017)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:98]
PARAGRAPH_159572: Consumer's liability for unauthorised use of credit card or other identifier providing access to credit

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:98]
PARAGRAPH_159573: A consumer who has concluded a credit agreement with a creditor is liable for the unauthorised use of a credit card or another identifier providing access to credit only if the unauthorised use is due to the consumer having:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:98]
PARAGRAPH_159574: 1) surrendered the identifier to a person unauthorised to use it;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:98]
PARAGRAPH_159575: 2) acted negligently; or

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:98]
PARAGRAPH_159576: 3) failed to notify the creditor of the loss, unauthorised possession or unauthorised use of the identifier without undue delay once having detected this.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:98]
PARAGRAPH_159577: In the cases referred to in subsection 1, paragraphs 2 and 3, the consumer is liable for the unauthorised use of the identifier for a maximum of EUR 50. This limitation does not, however, apply if the consumer has acted with intent or gross negligence.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:98]
PARAGRAPH_159578: The consumer is not, however, liable for the unauthorised use of the identifier:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:98]
PARAGRAPH_159579: 1) to the extent that the identifier has been used after the creditor was informed of the loss, unauthorised possession or unauthorised use of the identifier;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:98] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159580: 2) if the creditor has failed to ensure that the holder of the identifier has the opportunity to fulfil their notification obligation in accordance with subsection 1, paragraph 3;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:98]
PARAGRAPH_159581: 3) if the seller or the service provider or the person who as their representative has received the identifier has not appropriately ensured the holder's right to use the identifier; or

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:98]
PARAGRAPH_159582: 4) if the creditor has not required that the identity of the consumer be verified when using the identifier in the manner laid down in section 15, subsection 1.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:99]
PARAGRAPH_159583: Notwithstanding the provisions of subsection 3, the consumer is liable for the unauthorised use of the identifier if the consumer or another holder of the identifier has intentionally submitted a false notification or otherwise acted fraudulently.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:99]
PARAGRAPH_159584: Provisions on certain credit types

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:99]
PARAGRAPH_159585: Section 41 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:99]
PARAGRAPH_159586: Prior information

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:99] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159587: As regards consumer credit linked to a current account the contractual terms of which provide that the credit period is a maximum of three months or that the credit must be repaid on demand, the creditor and the credit intermediary shall, in addition to provisions laid down elsewhere by law on the obligation to provide information, provide the consumer with information on the following before the conclusion of the credit agreement:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:99]
PARAGRAPH_159588: 1) the creditor;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:99]
PARAGRAPH_159589: 2) the credit offered, the costs of credit and the repayment of the credit;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:99]
PARAGRAPH_159590: 3) the consequences of a breach of agreement;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:99]
PARAGRAPH_159591: 4) the consumer's legal rights.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:99]
PARAGRAPH_159592: The provisions of subsection 1 on information to be provided before the conclusion of the agreement also apply if the creditor enters into a payment arrangement agreement with the consumer due to the consumer's payment difficulties, the terms of which are not less favourable to the consumer than the initial credit agreement.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:99]
PARAGRAPH_159593: Further provisions on the information to be provided are laid down by Government Decree.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:99]
PARAGRAPH_159594: Section 42 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:99]
PARAGRAPH_159595: Provision of prior information over the telephone

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:99] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159596: If the consumer requests over the telephone for immediate access to credit referred to in section 41, subsection 1, the consumer shall be provided with the information laid down in chapter 6a, section 10, subsection 1 and subsection 2, paragraphs 1 and 3-6 as well as the information on the credit offered and its repayment. Further provisions on the information to be provided are laid down by Government Decree.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:100]
PARAGRAPH_159597: The provisions of subsection 1 apply also if the consumer requests over the telephone that a payment arrangement agreement referred to in section 41, subsection 2 be concluded.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:100]
PARAGRAPH_159598: Section 43 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:100]
PARAGRAPH_159599: Provision of prior information on durable medium

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:100] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159600: The prior information referred to in section 41 above shall be provided to the consumer in good time before the conclusion of the agreement using the European Consumer Credit Information Form for specific types of credit or another durable medium as the creditor or the credit intermediary may decide. Further provisions on the form are laid down by Government Decree.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:100] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159601: If the agreement is concluded at the consumer's request over the telephone or using such a means of distance communication which does not enable providing the prior information on a durable medium before the conclusion of the agreement, the creditor shall provide the information in accordance with section 45 without delay after the conclusion of the agreement.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:100] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159602: The consumer shall, in addition, be supplied on request and free of charge, with a copy of the draft credit agreement.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:100]
PARAGRAPH_159603: Section 44 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:100]
PARAGRAPH_159604: Exception concerning credit intermediaries acting in ancillary capacity

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:100]
PARAGRAPH_159605: The provisions of sections 41-43 on the credit intermediary's obligation to provide the consumer with information do not, however, apply to sellers or service providers acting as credit intermediaries in an ancillary capacity alongside their primary activity.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:100]
PARAGRAPH_159606: Section 45 (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:100]
PARAGRAPH_159607: Credit agreements linked to current account

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:100] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159608: A consumer credit agreement linked to a current account the contractual terms of which provide that the credit period is a maximum of three months or that the credit must be repaid on demand shall be concluded in writing and the consumer shall be provided with a copy of the agreement. The agreement may also be concluded electronically in a way that allows the unchanged storage and replication of the agreement by the consumer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:100] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_159609: The agreement shall provide information on the following:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:100]
PARAGRAPH_159610: 1) the parties to the credit agreement;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:100]
PARAGRAPH_159611: 2) the credit offered, the costs of credit and the repayment of the credit;
