The provisions of sections 75-78 of the Sale of Goods Act do not apply to the sale of elements referred to in this chapter if the compensation to be received by the contractor under those provisions would exceed the compensation under sections 28-30 of this chapter when the contract is terminated by the contractor.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:148]
PARAGRAPH_160224: Section 33 (16/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:148]
PARAGRAPH_160225: Limitation of loss or damage and adjustment of damages

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:148]
PARAGRAPH_160226: The provisions of chapter 5, section 30 apply correspondingly in the case of a contract referred to in this chapter.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:148]
PARAGRAPH_160227: Section 34 (16/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:148]
PARAGRAPH_160228: Liability in damages of parties other than contractor

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:148]
PARAGRAPH_160229: The provisions of chapter 5, section 31 and chapter 8, sections 34 or 35 on the buyer's or customer's right to direct their claim based on a lack of conformity also against a trader in a previous link in the chain of transactions or against a trader whose assistance the contractor has enlisted apply correspondingly to contracts referred to in this chapter.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:148]
PARAGRAPH_160230: Section 35 (572/2020)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:148]
PARAGRAPH_160231: Penalty fee

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:148]
PARAGRAPH_160232: Provisions on penalty fees imposed for violations of provisions of section 25, subsection 2 of this chapter are laid down in the Act on Certain Powers of the Consumer Protection Authorities.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:148]
PARAGRAPH_160233: Chapter 10 (227/2011)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:148]
PARAGRAPH_160234: Timeshare and long-term holiday products

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:148]
PARAGRAPH_160235: Section 1 (227/2011)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:148]
PARAGRAPH_160236: Scope of application

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:148]
PARAGRAPH_160237: This chapter lays down provisions on contracts between a trader and a consumer on the sale or intermediation of a timeshare or a long-term holiday product or the exchange of a timeshare. In addition, provisions are laid down on the marketing by traders to consumers of timeshares, long- term holiday products and related intermediation or exchange activity.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:148]
PARAGRAPH_160238: The provisions of the chapter do not apply to contracts for no consideration or for timeshare and long-term holiday product contracts concluded for a fixed term of no more than one year. The provisions do, however, apply if the period of validity of a fixed-term timeshare or long-term holiday product contract may be extended for more than one year without any separate agreement between the parties on the extension.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:148]
PARAGRAPH_160239: Section 2 (227/2011)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:148]
PARAGRAPH_160240: Definitions

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:148]
PARAGRAPH_160241: For the purposes of this chapter:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:149]
PARAGRAPH_160242: 1) timeshare means the right, divided into periods of time repeated as determined in the contract, to use accommodation linked with immovable or movable property;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:149]
PARAGRAPH_160243: 2) timeshare unit means a building or unit intended for residential use the right to use of which is based on timeshares;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:149]
PARAGRAPH_160244: 3) long-term holiday product means a right of a duration of more than one year primarily to obtain a discount or other benefit in respect of accommodation either in isolation or linked with travel or other services;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:149]
PARAGRAPH_160245: 4) exchange contract means a contract for joining an exchange system which allows a timeshare owner to have access to other accommodation or services covered by the system;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:149]
PARAGRAPH_160246: 5) intermediation contract means a sale or purchase assignment concerning a timeshare or long- term holiday product;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:149]
PARAGRAPH_160247: 6) ancillary contract means a contract related to a timeshare contract or long-term holiday product contract for services provided by a trader or a third party on the basis of a contract or other arrangement between that third party and the trader;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:149]
PARAGRAPH_160248: 7) provision of information on a durable medium means the provision of information personally on paper or electronically in a way that allows the unchanged storage and replication of the information by the recipient.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:149]
PARAGRAPH_160249: Section 3 (227/2011)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:149]
PARAGRAPH_160250: Mandatory nature of provisions and application of foreign law

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:149]
PARAGRAPH_160251: Any contractual term deviating from the provisions of this chapter to the detriment of the consumer is null and void unless otherwise provided below.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:149]
PARAGRAPH_160252: If any of the immovable properties to which the contract pertains is situated in a Member State of the European Economic Area (EEA State) and the law of a non-EEA State would become applicable to the contract, the provisions of this chapter apply, however, to the extent that the consumer is provided with more effective protection under them than under the law otherwise applied. The provisions apply correspondingly also to another contract within the scope of application of this chapter if the trader pursues commercial or professional activities in an EEA State or, by any means, directs such activities to an EEA State and the contract falls within the scope of such activities.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:150]
PARAGRAPH_160253: Section 4 (227/2011)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:150]
PARAGRAPH_160254: Prior information

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:150] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_160255: The trader shall, in good time before the consumer concludes a contract within the scope of application of this chapter or makes a binding offer concerning it, provide the consumer with clear and sufficiently detailed information on:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:150]
PARAGRAPH_160256: 1) the trader that is party to the contract;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:150]
PARAGRAPH_160257: 2) the nature, content and use of the rights which are the subject of the contract;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:150]
PARAGRAPH_160258: 3) the price, other payments and costs;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:150]
PARAGRAPH_160259: 4) the immovable property, building, unit or other accommodation to which the right to use under the contract pertains;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:150]
PARAGRAPH_160260: 5) the services included in the contract;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:150]
PARAGRAPH_160261: 6) the right of withdrawal under section 9 and the ban on advance payments under section 12;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:150]
PARAGRAPH_160262: 7) the duration of the contract and the termination or other cessation of the contract;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:150]
PARAGRAPH_160263: 8) the possibility of referring a dispute concerning the contract for settlement by the Consumer Disputes Board or another equivalent body handling consumer disputes.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:150] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_160264: The information referred to in subsection 1 above shall be provided on the timeshare, long-term holiday product, intermediation contract or exchange contract in the standard information form set out separately for each type of contract. The form shall be provided free of charge on a durable medium and, at the choice of the consumer, in the language of the state in which the consumer is a resident or a national in the case of an EEA State and if the chosen language is an official language of the European Union or Norwegian or Icelandic.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:150]
PARAGRAPH_160265: Further provisions on the format and contents of the information forms are laid down by decree of the Ministry of Justice.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:150]
PARAGRAPH_160266: Section 5 (227/2011)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:150] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_160268: When marketing rights or activities falling within the scope of application of this chapter, the trader shall provide information on the information form referred to in section 4 and on where and how the consumer can obtain it.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:151] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_160269: If a contract is offered to a consumer personally at a promotion or sales event, the trader shall clearly indicate in the invitation to the event the nature and the commercial purpose of the event. The information form referred to in section 4 shall be available to the consumer at any time during the event.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:151] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_160270: A timeshare or a long-term holiday product shall not be marketed as an investment.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:151]
PARAGRAPH_160271: Section 6 (227/2011)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:151]
PARAGRAPH_160272: Format and language of contract

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:151] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_160273: The contract shall be concluded in writing and signed by the parties. The consumer shall receive a copy of the contract. The agreement may also be concluded electronically in a way that allows the unchanged storage and replication of the agreement by the consumer. The provisions of the Act on Strong Electronic Identification and Electronic Trust Services apply to signing contracts electronically. Provisions on the format and contents of any credit agreement linked to the principal agreement are laid down in chapter 7 of this Act.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:151] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_160274: The contract shall be concluded, at the choice of the consumer, in the language of the state in which the consumer is a resident or a national in the case of an EEA State and if the chosen language is an official language of the European Union or Norwegian or Icelandic. If the immovable property to which the contract pertains is situated in an EEA State other than a state in the language of which the contract is concluded, the trader shall, in addition, provide the consumer with a certified translation of the contract in a language of the state in which the property is situated. If the contract is concluded with a trader operating in Finland in a language other than Finnish or Swedish, the trader shall, at the consumer's request and at the choice of the consumer, provide the consumer with a translation of the contract in Finnish or Swedish.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:151]
PARAGRAPH_160275: Section 7 (227/2011)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:151]
PARAGRAPH_160276: Contents of contract

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:151] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_160277: The information provided in the information form referred to in section 4 forms a part of the contract unless the parties separately agree otherwise. The trader shall not unilaterally alter the information provided in the form unless the changes result from unusual and unforeseeable circumstances beyond the trader's control, the consequences of which could not have been avoided even if all due care had been exercised. Any changes shall be communicated to the consumer on a durable medium before the contract is concluded. The information in the form and any changes to it shall be mentioned in the contract. In addition, the contract shall mention the name and address of each of the parties and the date and place of the conclusion of the contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:152] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_160278: The contract shall be accompanied by a separate standard form the consumer can use to notify of withdrawal from the contract in accordance with section 9. Provisions on the form and contents of the withdrawal form are laid down by decree of the Ministry of Justice.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:152]
PARAGRAPH_160279: Section 8 (227/2011)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:152]
PARAGRAPH_160280: Other requirements concerning conclusion of contract

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:152] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_160281: Before the conclusion of the contract, the trader shall draw the consumer's attention particularly to the existence of the right of withdrawal and the withdrawal period under section 9 and to the ban on advance payments during the withdrawal period under section 12. The trader shall ensure that the consumer signs the contractual terms corresponding to these provisions separately.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:152]
PARAGRAPH_160282: Section 9 (227/2011)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:152]
PARAGRAPH_160283: Right of withdrawal

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:152]
PARAGRAPH_160284: The consumer has the right to withdraw from the contract within 14 days from the conclusion of the contract or from a later date on which the consumer received a copy of the contract. If the consumer is offered an exchange contract in conjunction with a timeshare contract, the withdrawal period concerning the timeshare contract applies to both contracts.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:152] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_160285: The consumer shall notify the trader of withdrawal using the withdrawal form referred to in section 7, subsection 2 or another durable medium.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:152] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_160286: The exercise of the right of withdrawal by the consumer terminates the obligations of the parties to perform the contract. The consumer shall not be required to compensate for any costs incurred by the trader from the withdrawal or for any service performed before withdrawal. The trader shall reimburse any payments received by the trader from the consumer without delay. Interest shall be paid on the amounts reimbursed in accordance with the interest rate referred to in section 3, subsection 2 of the Interest Act from the date on which the payment was received.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:152]
PARAGRAPH_160287: Section 10 (227/2011)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:152]
PARAGRAPH_160288: Impact on withdrawal period of failure to provide form

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:152]
PARAGRAPH_160289: If the trader has failed to provide the consumer with the withdrawal form referred to in section 7, subsection 2 attached to the contract or otherwise on a durable medium, the withdrawal period expires after one year and 14 days from the date referred to in section 9, subsection 1. If the withdrawal form is provided within that year, the withdrawal period of 14 days starts from the day the consumer receives the form.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:153]
PARAGRAPH_160290: If the consumer has not been provided with the information form referred to in section 4 on a durable medium, the withdrawal period expires after three months and 14 days from the date referred to in section 9, subsection 1. If the information form is provided within those three months, the withdrawal period of 14 days starts from the day the consumer receives the form.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:153]
PARAGRAPH_160291: Section 11 (227/2011)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:153]
PARAGRAPH_160292: Termination of ancillary contract and credit agreement

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:153]
PARAGRAPH_160293: If the consumer withdraws from a principal contract concerning a timeshare or a long-term holiday product, any intermediation contract or other ancillary contract linked to it is terminated automatically and without consequences to the consumer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:153]
PARAGRAPH_160294: If the consumer has been granted credit for the principal contract by the trader by themselves or by another trader under a contract or another consumer credit provision arrangement concluded with the trader, the credit agreement is terminated when the consumer withdraws from the principal contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:153]
PARAGRAPH_160295: Section 12 (227/2011)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:153]
PARAGRAPH_160296: Ban on receiving payments during withdrawal period and period of validity of intermediation contract

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:153] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_160297: The trader or any third party shall not receive any payment from the consumer based on a timeshare contract, long-term holiday product contract or intermediation contract before the expiry of the withdrawal period in accordance with section 9 or 10. The ban also applies to the provision of any payment commitment, surety or other security or any other arrangement that may place the consumer under a payment obligation.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:153]
PARAGRAPH_160298: The ban on the consumer's advance payments and other commitments and arrangements in accordance with subsection 1 applies to an intermediation contract until the intermediation task has been carried out or the intermediation contract has otherwise ended.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:153]
PARAGRAPH_160299: Section 13 (227/2011)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:153]
PARAGRAPH_160300: Payment schedule for long-term holiday product and termination of contract

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:153] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_160301: The trader shall prepare a payment schedule, for the payments in accordance with a long-term holiday product contract, where the payments, including any membership fee, payable by the consumer are divided into yearly instalments, each of which are of equal value. No other payments in addition to the payment instalments specified in the payment schedule shall be required from the consumer. The trader shall send the consumer an invoice or other request for payment on a durable medium at least 14 days in advance of each due date.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:154]
PARAGRAPH_160302: From the second instalment payment onwards, the consumer may terminate a long-term holiday product contract without incurring any penalty by giving notice to the trader within fourteen calendar days from receiving the request for payment of the instalment for that year.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:154]
PARAGRAPH_160303: Section 14 (227/2011)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:154]
PARAGRAPH_160304: Payment of timeshare unit price during construction period

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:154] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_160305: If it is agreed that some part of the price of a timeshare unit is to be paid before the building control authority has accepted the housing unit for use, the amounts of any advance instalments of the price of the unit shall not be so large that they are disproportionate to the value of the trader's performance during the period within which the instalments fall due. At least ten per cent of the price of the unit may be required to be paid only once the housing unit has been accepted for use and the consumer has had a reasonable opportunity to inspect it.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:154]
PARAGRAPH_160306: Section 15 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:154]
PARAGRAPH_160307: Application of provisions concerning sale of goods

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:154]
PARAGRAPH_160308: The provisions of chapter 5 on the sale of goods apply, where appropriate, also to a timeshare contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:154]
PARAGRAPH_160309: Section 16 (227/2011)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:154]
PARAGRAPH_160310: Consequences of violations of certain provisions

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:154]
PARAGRAPH_160311: Where necessary for consumer protection, a prohibitory injunction may be imposed on a trader that violates the provisions of sections 4-8 or 12-14 of this chapter on marketing and contractual relationship of this chapter to refrain from continuing or repeating such a practice or a comparable practice. Provisions on the imposition of a prohibitory injunction and its enforcement by a notice of a conditional fine are laid down in chapters 2 and 3.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:154]
PARAGRAPH_160312: Provisions on penalty fees imposed for violations of provisions of section 4 and 5; section 9, subsection 1; and section 12 of this chapter are laid down in the Act on Certain Powers of the Consumer Protection Authorities. (572/2020)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:154]
PARAGRAPH_160313: Chapter 11 (746/2010) (746/2010)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:154]
PARAGRAPH_160314: Chapter 11 was repealed by Act 746/2010.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:154]
PARAGRAPH_160315: Chapter 12

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:155]
PARAGRAPH_160316: Miscellaneous provisions

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:155]
PARAGRAPH_160317: Section 1 (1242/2021)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:155]
PARAGRAPH_160318: Liability of intermediary of consumer goods or services

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:155]
PARAGRAPH_160319: A trader who intermediates a contract for consumer goods or services on behalf of a party offering the goods or services is liable to the consumer acquiring the goods or services for the performance of the contract in accordance with chapters 5, 5a and 8. This liability does not, however, arise if the intermediary is acting on behalf of another trader and the consumer was aware of this and of the impacts of this on their rights at the time of the conclusion of the contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:155]
PARAGRAPH_160320: The intermediary's liability does not limit the consumer's rights in relation to another party to the contract.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:155]
PARAGRAPH_160321: The provisions laid down separately on the liability of real estate agents apply to the liability of real estate agents.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:155]
PARAGRAPH_160322: Section 1a (16/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:155]
PARAGRAPH_160323: Claim period concerning damages in certain cases

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:155] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_160324: Any claim based on this Act concerning compensation for damage to property caused by a lack of conformity in goods, or compensation for damage to property caused by a lack of conformity in material used in service performance, to property other than the object of service shall be filed within three years from the date on which the claimant was informed of the lack of conformity having become apparent and of the party liable to compensate. The claim shall, however, be filed within ten years from the date on which the party liable to compensate put the goods or material causing the damage into circulation.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:155]
PARAGRAPH_160325: Section 1b (16/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:155]
PARAGRAPH_160326: Relationship with Tort Liability Act and other acts

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:155]
PARAGRAPH_160327: The provisions of this Act do not restrict the right of a person suffering loss, injury or damage to claim for compensation under the Tort Liability Act (412/1974), the Product Liability Act or another act.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:155]
PARAGRAPH_160328: Section 1c (1211/2013)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:155]
PARAGRAPH_160329: Right to rely on certain notifications and documents

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:155]
PARAGRAPH_160330: If a notification of lack of conformity or a notification of termination or withdrawal of contract referred to in this Act has been sent to the recipient in an appropriate manner, the sender may rely on the notification even if it is late, distorted or undelivered.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:156]
PARAGRAPH_160331: If no other evidence can be provided for the date on which a notification was received, notifications sent by post are deemed to have been received on the seventh day after they were sent and notifications sent electronically on the day they were sent.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:156]
PARAGRAPH_160332: The provisions of subsections 1 and 2 on notifications also apply to confirmations, contractual terms and other documents that a trader has sent in accordance with this Act to a consumer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:156]
PARAGRAPH_160333: Section 1d (16/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:156]
PARAGRAPH_160334: Handling of disputes

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:156] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_160335: A term of a contract, concluded before the materialisation of a dispute, under which disputes between the trader and the consumer must be settled by arbitration is not binding on the consumer.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:156]
PARAGRAPH_160336: Provisions on the competent court and the choice of court agreement are laid down in chapter 10 of the Code of Judicial Procedure (4/1743). (140/2009)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:156]
PARAGRAPH_160337: Section 1e (29/2005)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:156]
PARAGRAPH_160338: Calculation of time limit

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:156] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_160339: In calculating a time limit laid down in this Act, the day on which the contract was concluded or other similar measure was carried out and from which the time limit begins is not taken into account. If the last day of a time limit is a Sunday, public holiday, the Independence Day, the First of May, Christmas Eve, Midsummer Eve or a Saturday, a measure to be carried out within the time limit may still be carried out on the first business day after that.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:156]
PARAGRAPH_160340: Section 1f (416/1999)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:156]
PARAGRAPH_160341: General choice-of-law provisions

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:156]
PARAGRAPH_160342: Unless otherwise provided by the provisions of this Act or another act, the law applicable to contractual obligations referred to this Act is determined in accordance with the Rome Convention of 19 June 1980 on the Law Applicable to Contractual Obligations. Even where the contractual obligations referred to in this Act do not fall within the scope of application of the said Convention, the rules of the Convention are complied with as appropriate.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:156]
PARAGRAPH_160344: Further provisions (16/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:156]
PARAGRAPH_160345: Further provisions on the application and implementation of this Act may be issued by decree.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:156]
PARAGRAPH_160346: Section 3 Entry into force (16/1994)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:FINLAND] [CATEGORY:NATIONAL_LAWS] [PAGE:157]
PARAGRAPH_160347: This Act enters into force on 1 September 1978.
